### [135] [Large Language Models Are Overconfident in Their Own Responses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03437)
*Mario Sanz-Guerrero,Manuel Mager,Katharina von der Wense*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了对话型大语言模型在指令微调后校准能力下降的问题，发现聊天模板会通过‘所有权偏差’加剧这一问题：模型对自己生成的回答比对用户相同回答更自信。实验表明，模型对自己的回答信心最高可高出26%。为此，作者提出一种推理时的简单策略——将模型的回答伪装成用户输入以进行置信度评估，该方法无需重新训练即可显著降低过度自信，使指令微调模型的校准性能提升26%，缩小与基础模型的差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究表明，指令微调的大语言模型校准能力弱于其基础预训练版本，但聊天模板对校准的影响尚不明确。本文旨在揭示指令微调与聊天格式各自对模型校准的影响机制，尤其是后者是否加剧了校准偏差。

Method: 通过解耦后训练算法与聊天格式的影响，系统地分析不同因素对模型置信度的影响；设计实验比较模型对自己回答与用户相同回答的置信度差异，识别出‘所有权偏差’现象；提出一种推理时的简单修正策略，即在置信度评估阶段将模型输出视为用户输入，从而抑制过度自信。

Result: 实验结果显示，模型对自己生成的回答置信度比对相同内容的用户回答高最多达26%；采用提出的推理时策略后，模型校准性能显著改善，过自信现象减轻，校准误差降低26%，且无需重新训练。

Conclusion: 聊天模板通过引入‘所有权偏差’进一步恶化了指令微调模型的校准问题。通过在置信度评估阶段将模型输出视为用户输入，可在不改变模型参数的情况下有效缓解过自信，显著提升校准性能，使指令微调模型的表现更接近基础模型。

Abstract: Prior work has shown that instruction-tuned large language models (LLMs) are less well calibrated than their base pre-trained counterparts. However, little is known about the frequently used chat template's effect on the calibration of conversational LLMs. In this work, we investigate the mechanisms driving this miscalibration by decoupling the effects of the post-training algorithm and the chat format. We find that, while instruction tuning fundamentally harms calibration, the chat template aggravates the issue through an "ownership bias" -- models are significantly more confident in their own answers than in identical answers provided by a user. Extensive experiments across six recent open-weight LLMs, three benchmarks, and three confidence elicitation methods show that models assign up to 26% higher confidence to their own responses. Leveraging this insight, we propose a simple inference-time strategy: framing the model's answer as user input during confidence elicitation. This approach significantly reduces overconfidence and improves calibration by up to 26% without the need for retraining, narrowing the gap between base and instruction-tuned models.

*Anling Xiang,Yuwen Yang,Yang Shen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: AutoTail-BSFGM是一种针对中文学术语料中类别不平衡和语义相近标签问题的类平衡感知微调方法，结合了自动门控尾部优先调整、弱平衡Softmax辅助损失和快速梯度法对抗正则化。该方法仅改变训练目标与流程，推理阶段仍使用基础大小的编码器和线性分类器。在两个基于CSL的任务上评估：67类的摘要到学科任务和13类的标题到类别任务。在主要摘要任务上，该方法在Chinese RoBERTa-WWM和MacBERT-base上均提升了验证集和锁箱集准确率；使用MacBERT-base时，验证准确率提升0.83个百分点，锁箱准确率提升0.49个百分点，配对McNemar检验显示显著性（p=0.023）。在标题任务上，验证准确率提升0.70点，验证平衡准确率提升2.64点；锁箱准确率基本不变，但锁箱平衡准确率提升1.22点。结果表明，该方法在改善类别平衡敏感行为方面有有限但一致的增益，尤其适用于基于摘要的学术分类任务。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出AutoTail-BSFGM，融合自动门控尾部优先调整、弱平衡Softmax辅助损失和快速梯度法对抗正则化，仅修改训练目标与过程，保持推理结构不变。

Abstract: Scholarly text classification supports literature organization, subject indexing, and research intelligence, but Chinese scholarly corpora often contain imbalanced and semantically adjacent disciplinary labels. We propose AutoTail-BSFGM, a class-balance-aware fine-tuning method that combines an automatically gated tail-prior adjustment, a weak Balanced Softmax auxiliary loss, and Fast Gradient Method adversarial regularization. The method changes only the training objective and procedure; inference uses the same single base-size encoder and linear classifier as the corresponding label-smoothed baseline. On the title task, the method improves validation accuracy by 0.70 points and validation balanced accuracy by 2.64 points; lockbox accuracy is approximately neutral while lockbox balanced accuracy improves by 1.22 points. The results support a bounded contribution: AutoTail-BSFGM improves class-balance-sensitive behavior and yields consistent gains for abstract-based scholarly classification, without uniformly improving every metric on every split.

### [138] [Beyond the Literal: Decomposing Pragmatic Intent in Multimodal Meme Understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03604)
*Zhengyi Zhao,Shubo Zhang,Zezhong Wang,Luyao Ye,Huimin Wang,Hanqi Yan,Binyang Li,Kam-Fai Wong,Yulan He*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出一种名为意图投影（Intent Projection）的框架，旨在解决大型视觉语言模型在理解梗图和讽刺内容时容易陷入字面意义的问题。通过在表示、输出和目标三个层面分离字面与语用信息，模型能够更准确地捕捉作者的真实意图。具体方法包括：使用正交投影模块去除图像-文本融合表示中的主导单模态特征，保留语用残差；引入表面真实情感分类器以锚定解码器的极性差异标签；外部化结构化推理链；并采用对比奖励机制惩罚重复字面描述的答案。在六个多模态基准测试中，该方法显著优于开源基线，并缩小了与专有模型之间的差距，尤其在高分歧性内容上表现突出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型视觉语言模型在处理梗图和讽刺内容时，常将图像的字面描述误认为其真正含义，导致语用理解偏差。标准指令微调使字面内容与语用意义混淆，使得表面细节干扰最终输出。因此需要一种方法来明确区分字面与语用信息，提升对隐含意图的理解能力。

Method: 提出意图投影框架，从表示、输出和目标三个层面实现字面与语用的分解：1）在表示层面，使用正交投影模块移除融合表示中的主导单模态方向，保留语用残差；2）在输出层面，生成结构化推理链；3）在目标层面，设计对比奖励机制，惩罚重复字面描述的回答。同时引入表面真实情感分类器，为解码器提供极性差异的离散标签。

Result: 在六个多模态基准测试中，意图投影框架显著优于现有开源基线模型，特别是在高语义分歧的梗图上提升明显，大幅缩小了与专有模型的性能差距，证明了其在复杂语用理解任务中的有效性。

Conclusion: 意图投影通过系统性地分离字面与语用信号，在多个挑战性任务上实现了卓越的性能，为提升大模型对讽刺、隐喻等复杂表达的理解能力提供了有效路径。

Abstract: When asked what a meme or sarcastic post means, Large Vision Language Models (LVLMs) tend to describe what the image shows rather than what the author is trying to communicate. Standard instruction tuning entangles a post's literal content with its pragmatic meaning, letting surface-level details contaminate the final response. We reframe meme understanding as a problem of literal-pragmatic decomposition and propose \textbf{Intent Projection}, a framework that separates the two signals at the representation, output, and objective levels within a single LVLM backbone. At the representation level, an orthogonal projection module removes dominant unimodal directions from the fused image-text representation, retaining only the pragmatic residual, while a surface-real affect classifier anchors the decoder with a discrete tag that names the polarity gap. At the output level, the model externalizes a structured reasoning chain, and at the objective level a contrastive reward explicitly penalizes answers that restate the literal description. Across six multimodal benchmarks, Intent Projection consistently outperforms open-source baselines and narrows the gap to proprietary models, with the largest gains on high-divergence posts where literal collapse is most damaging.

### [139] [Building Reliable Long-Form Generation via Hallucination Rejection Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03628)
*Lin Li,Georgia Channing,Suhaas M Bhat,Gabriel Davis Jones,Yarin Gal*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为SHARS的推理阶段幻觉缓解框架，通过使用任意幻觉检测器识别并拒绝生成中的幻觉段落，进行重采样以生成忠实内容，有效缓解长文本生成中的幻觉累积问题。采用语义不确定性作为检测器，并进行了多项改进以适应长文本生成，无需外部资源即可实现自纠正，同时保持与外部知识源的兼容性。实验表明，该方法显著减少幻觉，且在信息量上表现不降反升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在开放文本生成中容易产生幻觉，尤其在长文本生成中，早期错误会不断传播和放大，严重影响可靠性。因此需要一种机制在生成过程中主动识别并消除幻觉，避免错误积累。

Method: 提出SHARS框架，利用任意幻觉检测器（如语义不确定性）识别生成中的幻觉段落，拒绝并重采样，仅保留高置信度内容，构建后续生成基础，从而抑制幻觉传播。对语义不确定性检测器进行了针对性改进以适配长文本生成。

Result: 在标准化幻觉基准测试中，该方法显著降低长文本生成中的幻觉率，同时保持或提升生成内容的信息量，且无需依赖外部资源，具备良好扩展性。

Conclusion: SHARS框架通过段落级幻觉拒绝采样，实现了无需外部知识源的自我纠正能力，在长文本生成中有效缓解了幻觉雪球效应，提升了生成内容的事实一致性与可靠性。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have achieved remarkable progress in open-ended text generation, yet they remain prone to hallucinating incorrect or unsupported content, which undermines their reliability. This issue is exacerbated in long-form generation due to hallucination snowballing, a phenomenon where early errors propagate and compound into subsequent outputs. To address this challenge, we propose a novel inference-time hallucination mitigation framework, named Segment-wise HAllucination Rejection Sampling (SHARS), which uses an arbitrary hallucination detector to identify and reject hallucinated segments during generation and resample until faithful content is produced. By retaining only confident information and building subsequent generations upon it, the framework mitigates hallucination accumulation and enhances factual consistency. To instantiate this framework, we adopt semantic uncertainty as the detector and introduce several vital modifications to address its limitations and better adapt it to long-form text. Our method enables models to self-correct hallucinations without requiring external resources such as web search or knowledge bases, while remaining compatible with them for future extensions. Empirical evaluations on standardized hallucination benchmarks demonstrate that our method substantially reduces hallucinations in long-form generation while preserving or even improving the informativeness of generation. Code is available at: https://github.com/TreeLLi/hallucination-rejection-sampling.

### [140] [Safety Measurements for Fine-tuned LLMs Should be Grounded in Capability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03648)
*Krishnapriya Vishnubhotla,Hillary Dawkins,Isar Nejadgholi,Svetlana Kiritchenko*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究聚焦于微调对大语言模型安全性的影响，强调以特定能力目标为锚点进行微调，以避免随意的实验选择。通过多维度评估，发现微调可能导致模型在安全提示下生成不连贯内容，自动化安全判断对这类输出不可靠，且不同安全基准和评估者会得出不同结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对微调影响模型安全性的评估多基于有限且随机的实验设置，缺乏系统性和可比性。为获得有意义的结论并有效比较缓解方法，需将微调与具体能力目标相结合。

Method: 采用多维度评估方法，围绕特定能力目标进行微调，并在不同安全基准和评估者下测试模型行为，分析微调对模型安全性和生成质量的影响。

Result: 微调后的模型在面对安全提示时可能产生不连贯输出；自动化安全评估对不连贯输出不可靠；安全结论受所选基准和评估者影响显著。

Conclusion: 微调应以明确的能力目标为导向，否则可能导致安全评估结果失真。必须谨慎选择评估基准和评估方式，以确保对模型安全性的可靠判断。

Abstract: Adapting foundation large language models to a user's task or preferred style through fine-tuning can result in compromising the model's safety. Previous works examined the effects of fine-tuning on model safety in limited and seemingly random experimental settings. We argue that anchoring fine-tuning to a specific capability goal is essential for avoiding arbitrary empirical choices, allowing us to draw meaningful conclusions about safety impacts, and to compare mitigation methods on a consistent basis. We conduct a multi-dimensional evaluation of the effects of fine-tuning on model behavior by focusing on capability as well as safety. Our results surface important issues that (1) fine-tuned models can produce incoherent generations in response to safety prompts, (2) automated safety judgments are unreliable for such incoherent outputs, and (3) the conclusions about the effects of fine-tuning can change depending on the choice of safety benchmark as well as the safety evaluator.

### [141] [CoEval: Ranking Language Models for Custom Tasks Without Labeled Data or Trustworthy Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03650)
*Alexander Apartsin,Yehudit Aperstein*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CoEval 是一个开源、可复用的框架，用于在无任务特定标注数据且公共基准不可靠的情况下，对语言模型进行选择或排序。它通过教师模型自动生成无污染、属性可控的新基准，并使用跨家族判别器集成进行无标签评判，无需人类校准。该方法在真实情况验证下表现优异（准确率0.86），判别器组合比单一判别器更可靠，且生成内容与现有基准无重复。四任务实验共完成7978次评估，成本仅5.89美元。该流程可应用于任意领域，支持每次模型发布时重新运行，实现低成本、无污染的自动评分系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当缺乏任务特定标注数据且标准公共基准可能因预训练数据泄露而不可信时，传统评估方法失效，导致无法有效选择或排名语言模型。需要一种不依赖人工标注、避免数据泄露、可重复生成的评估机制。

Method: CoEval 利用教师模型根据任务描述生成全新、属性可控的合成数据集，构建无污染基准；采用跨家族判别器集成进行无标签模型评估，通过多样性而非规模保障判断可靠性。整个流程为声明式管道，可重复执行。

Result: 在有真实标签的场景中，CoEval 能恢复真实模型排名，正确率达0.86；判别器集成始终可靠，单一判别器可能反相关；生成内容与五大公开基准无13-gram重复；四任务实验产出7978次评估，总成本仅5.89美元。

Conclusion: CoEval 提供了一种标签自由、污染自由、可重复的模型评估方案，适用于任何应用领域，能实现低成本、高可靠性的自动排行榜，支持持续迭代与模型发布后的即时评估。

Abstract: Choosing or ranking language models for a specific application is hardest when no task-specific labeled data exists, and standard public benchmarks cannot be trusted, their items having likely leaked into pretraining, so scores reflect memorization rather than fitness. We present CoEval, an open-source, reusable framework that closes this gap end to end: from only a description of a task or domain, teacher models synthesize a fresh, attribute-controlled benchmark with no human labels, contamination-free because items are generated anew on each run, and a cross-family judge ensemble ranks candidate models with no human raters. Validated where ground truth exists, CoEval recovers the true model ranking and tracks ground-truth correctness at ho=0.86. The label-free judging needs no human calibration because judge-panel composition (vendor diversity), not size, drives reliability: a small, well-chosen cross-family panel is most reliable, while a single judge can be anti-correlated with ground truth (judge-choice regret 0.35) and the ensemble never is. Generated items show zero verbatim 13-gram overlap with five major public benchmarks; the panel cancels verbosity bias and precludes same-family self-preference. A four-task study produced 7,978 evaluations for USD 5.89. The same declarative pipeline applies to any domain and is cheap enough to re-run on every model release: a label-free, contamination-free leaderboard any team can regenerate for its own application.

</details>

We also conduct an error analysis to identify failure modes of question answering, such as yes/no flips, laterality errors, and output-language mismatches. Our findings show that strong performance on English medical VQA benchmarks does not necessarily translate to robust behavior in Indonesian clinical contexts. We observe a performance gap of 8 to 25 percent between the English and Indonesian settings, depending on the evaluation metric. These results highlight the need for more inclusive multilingual evaluation of medical multimodal foundation models. The dataset is available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/Lab-IS/IndoRad-VQA.

### [143] [Don't Forget Your Embeddings: Robust Knowledge Erasure via Precise Editing of Embeddings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03695)
*Clara Haya Suslik,Or Shafran,Mor Geva*

TL;DR: 本文提出EMBER，一种基于稀疏矩阵分解的即插即用擦除模块，通过精准干预词嵌入层实现概念知识的可靠擦除。实验表明，EMBER显著提升现有方法的擦除效果与鲁棒性，减少重学恢复率至35%（此前为70%-76%），且对模型连贯性影响极小，证明嵌入层干预对稳健知识擦除至关重要。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出EMBER模块，利用稀疏矩阵分解从词嵌入中精准移除特定概念特征，作为可插拔组件增强现有擦除方法。

Result: 在Gemma-2-2B-it和Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct上验证，EMBER显著提升擦除精度与鲁棒性，重学恢复率下降50%，仅影响少量专属概念词，连贯性损失微小。

Conclusion: 嵌入层的精确干预是实现强健概念擦除的关键，现有方法可通过集成EMBER获得显著性能提升。

Abstract: As language models are increasingly deployed in real-world applications, the ability to erase specific knowledge from them becomes critical for safety and compliance. Prominent methods seek persistent removal by updating the model's parameters, yet the target knowledge often can be recovered through adversarial prompting or relearning. In this work, we hypothesize this limitation stems in part from existing methods overlooking the embedding layer. To address this, we introduce EMBedding ERasure (EMBER), a plug-n-play erasure module that leverages Sparse Matrix Factorization for precise erasure of concept-related features from token embeddings. Through comprehensive evaluations across diverse concepts on Gemma-2-2B-it and Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct, we find that augmenting existing methods with EMBER consistently improves erasure efficacy and specificity across task formats, with minimal coherence loss. Moreover, it dramatically improves robustness to relearning, reducing regained accuracy by up to 50%, limiting it to 35% on Llama compared to 70%-76% for prior methods. Further analysis shows that the coherence cost is localized, affecting only a small set of concept-exclusive tokens. Our work establishes that precise embedding-level intervention is necessary for robust concept erasure, and demonstrates that existing methods can benefit from such augmentation.

### [144] [Re-Ranking Through an Attribution Lens for Citation Quality in Legal QA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03728)
*Mohamed Hesham Elganayni,Selim Saleh*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种基于扰动归因分数的轻量级交叉编码器，用于法律问答系统中的段落重排序，以提升引用答案的忠实度和与专家答案的一致性。实验表明，相较于基于语义相似性的排名，该方法显著改善了检索效果，且不同模型训练的重排器虽独立训练但能收敛到共享的相关性信号，说明其具备跨模型迁移能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有法律问答系统依赖语义相似性进行段落检索，但研究表明语义相似性与实际引用相关性无关，导致检索效果不佳。因此需要更准确的重排序机制来提升生成答案的引用可信度。

Method: 使用扰动归因方法（如C-LIME）计算段落的重要性得分，训练一个轻量级交叉编码器作为重排序器，利用这些归因分数对候选段落进行再排序，从而优化语言模型生成时的输入内容。

Result: 在AQuAECHR基准上，该方法显著提升了引用忠实度和与黄金标准答案的对齐程度；两个独立模型训练的重排器表现出跨模型一致性，证明其能减少模型特异性噪声并产生共享的相关性信号，尽管同模型重排序仍更有效。

Conclusion: 基于扰动归因的训练信号是构建引用感知检索的有效、模型无关的方法，为法律问答系统中更可靠的引用生成提供了新路径。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation systems for legal question answering typically retrieve passages based on semantic similarity and provide them to a language model, which then generates cited answers. Prior work assumes that highly ranked passages are most likely to be usefully cited by the model. Perturbation-based attribution methods, such as C-LIME, have been used exclusively for post-hoc explanation. However, on the AQuAECHR benchmark, semantic similarity does not correlate with passage attribution. Within a retriever's candidate pool, similarity-based ranking performs worse than random selection at surfacing gold citation paragraphs. To address this limitation, a lightweight cross-encoder is trained on continuous perturbation-based attribution scores to re-rank passages prior to generation. This approach is evaluated on the AQuAECHR benchmark, using two language models and five-fold cross-validation. The re-ranker substantially improves citation faithfulness and alignment with gold expert answers. Notably, two re-rankers trained independently on different models converge beyond their raw attribution agreement. This finding indicates that the cross-encoder reduces model-specific noise and produces a shared relevance signal that partially transfers across models, although same-model re-ranking remains more effective. These results demonstrate that perturbation-based attribution provides a practical, model-agnostic training signal for citation-aware retrieval.

### [145] [Entropy Gate: Entropy Quenching for Near-Lossless Token Compression in LLM Pipelines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03739)
*Justice Owusu Agyemang,Jerry John Kponyo,Kwame Opuni-Boachie Obour Agyekum,Francisca Adoma Acheampong,Kwame Agyeman-Prempeh Agyekum,James Dzisi Gadze*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出熵门（Entropy Gate）框架，通过熵淬灭机制压缩大语言模型中的低信息量内容（如重复上下文、冗长回复），利用多因素信息能量 $E(t)$ 和自适应淬灭调度 $T(τ)$ 动态移除低生存概率的令牌，同时通过保真度门控确保语义保留。该方法在多个提示类别中实现40-60%的压缩率，结合上下文去重和输出侧压缩可达到88-96%的总压缩比，且为无状态、模型无关的OpenAI兼容代理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM管道在低信息内容上浪费大量令牌预算，如重复上下文、冗余表述和冗长响应，亟需高效压缩机制以提升效率并降低成本。

Method: 引入熵淬灭机制，基于统计、结构和位置因素构建令牌信息能量 $E(t)$，使用Boltzmann生存概率判断是否移除令牌；采用自适应温度调度 $T(τ) = T_0 / (1 + ατ)$ 和能量加权相似性保真度门控 $θ$ 控制压缩过程；通过能量平方放大增强压缩效果，并支持上下文去重与输出侧压缩。

Result: Phase 1启发式方法在五类提示中实现40-60%压缩率，保真度 $S_E > 0.80$；加入能量平方放大后提升至50-85%；上下文去重额外带来50-70%节省；整体组合压缩率达88-96%，适用于智能体工作负载；理论分析表明压缩逼近信息论极限。

Conclusion: Entropy Gate是一种高效、通用、可部署的令牌压缩框架，能显著减少大语言模型的计算开销，同时保持高语义保真度，具有广泛的应用潜力。

Abstract: LLM pipelines waste substantial token budgets on low-information content: repeated context, verbose responses, and redundant boilerplate. We introduce Entropy Gate, a token compression framework applying entropy quenching $-$ a thermodynamic process that progressively freezes out low-energy tokens while preserving semantic fidelity. Each token receives a multi-factor information energy $E(t)$ combining statistical, structural, and positional components. An adaptive quenching schedule $T(τ) = T_0 / (1 + ατ)$ removes tokens whose Boltzmann survival probability $p_i = \exp(-E_i / kT)$ falls below threshold, with a fidelity gate halting compression when energy-weighted similarity drops below $θ$. We prove token selection by descending $E(t)$ maximizes expected semantic preservation, that quenching produces nested survival sets, and that achievable compression approaches the information-theoretic limit $\text{CR} \to 1 - I(P; T)/H(P)$. A Phase 1 heuristic achieves 40-60% compression across five prompt categories while maintaining $S_E > 0.80$, with energy-squared amplification $E \to E^2$ adding 10-25 percentage points. Context deduplication adds 50-70% savings on repeated blocks. Output-side quenching, motivated by findings that brevity improves accuracy, further reduces response overhead. Combined with external memory, reduction composes multiplicatively to 88-96% for agentic workloads. The framework is stateless, model-agnostic, and deploys as an OpenAI-compatible HTTP proxy.

</details>


### [146] [Framing Migration News with LLMs: Structured CoT as a Support for Human Interpretation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03761)
*David Alonso del Barrio,Jing Wen,Daniel Gatica-Perez*

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了本地部署的开源大模型在迁移新闻框架分析中的应用，提出一种基于Llama3-8B的结构化思维链（SCoT）提示方法，通过分步推理增强可解释性，提升分类性能，并支持人工审计与反思。实验表明，该方法在单个GPU上可行，且人类评估显示模型推理被普遍认为逻辑合理，能引发对初始判断的反思，但也存在影响人类判断的风险。研究强调了负责任、可访问的计算工具在社会性媒体叙事研究中的重要性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于大语言模型的新闻框架分析方法依赖专有API和大型模型，存在数据隐私、可重复性和资源不平等等问题。学术研究团队需要准确、透明、可审计且资源友好的工具来分析迁移新闻的叙述方式。

Method: 提出结构化思维链（SCoT）提示方法，利用Llama3-8B模型进行分步推理，依据预定义的框架类别提供可追溯的解释，支持用户审计输出并探索替代解读。

Conclusion: 结构化推理可增强模型输出的可追溯性，促进批判性解读，但需警惕其对人类判断的隐性影响。本地部署与人机协同的设计为社会性媒体叙事研究提供了更公平、透明的计算工具路径。

Abstract: Frame analysis of migration news is a socially consequential task: media scholars and researchers who study how migration is narrated need tools that are not only accurate, but transparent, auditable, and accessible within the resource constraints typical of academic research groups. Existing LLM-based approaches rely on proprietary APIs and large models that raise concerns about data privacy, reproducibility and equitable access among media researchers. This work studies how a locally deployable open-source LLM can support interpretable frame analysis as an assistive tool. We introduce a Structured Chain-of-Thought (SCoT) prompting approach using Llama3-8B, enabling step-by-step justifications grounded in predefined framing categories. This structured design allows users to audit model outputs and examine alternative interpretations in a task that is inherently subjective. We evaluate our approach on a dataset of migration-related news and show that SCoT improves classification performance over zero-shot and few-shot baselines while remaining feasible on a single GPU. Then, we conduct a human-centered evaluation in which annotators assess the coherence and influence of "the model's reasoning". Results indicate that SCoT explanations are generally perceived as logical (mean score 4.1/5, though with notable variation across texts) and can prompt reflection on initial interpretations, even when disagreement persists. Our findings highlight both the potential and risks of LLM-assisted frame analysis. While structured reasoning can increase the traceability of model outputs and support critical interpretation, it can also influence human judgment in subtle ways. By enabling local deployment and emphasizing human-in-the-loop interaction, this work contributes to discussions on responsible and accessible computational tools for the study of socially impactful media narratives.

</details>


### [147] [HybridThinker: Efficient Chain-of-Thought Reasoning via Compressed Memory and Transient Thought Steps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03768)
*Xin Liu,Runsong Zhao,Xinyu Liu,Junhao Ruan,Pengcheng Huang,Shichao Dong,Chunyang Xiao,Chenglong Wang,Changliang Li,Jingbo Zhu,Tong Xiao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: HybridThinker提出一种新型的思维链压缩方法，通过在推理时临时保留部分思考步骤并结合混合训练策略，有效缓解了传统压缩方法因信息丢失导致的错误累积问题。该方法在保持低推理开销的同时显著提升了模型性能，平均准确率提升5.8点，优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有思维链（CoT）压缩方法虽降低了计算和内存开销，但因丢失细粒度信息导致后续推理错误增多。如何在压缩的同时保留必要细节，是提升推理准确性的关键挑战。

Method: 提出HybridThinker框架，结合临时保留部分思考步骤与混合训练机制：训练时仅部分思考步骤可被注意力访问，其余被掩码，强制模型依赖记忆令牌进行信息压缩与检索，从而增强其压缩能力。

Result: 在4个推理基准测试中，HybridThinker达到与未压缩基线相当的性能，平均准确率提升5.8点，且推理时间相近；消融实验验证了临时保留与混合训练策略的有效性。

Conclusion: HybridThinker通过引入临时思考步骤保留与混合训练机制，在不增加推理成本的前提下显著提升了思维链压缩的效果，为高效、高精度的大语言模型推理提供了新范式。

Abstract: Extended chain-of-thought (CoT) traces improve LLM reasoning but incur substantial computational and memory costs. While existing CoT compression methods mitigate this by condensing thought steps into compact representations via memory tokens and retaining only these representations at inference time, the loss of fine-grained information makes subsequent steps more error-prone. To alleviate this, we propose \textbf{HybridThinker}, where in addition to preserved these representations, thought steps are also temporarily retained to provide fine-grained details. However, we observe that naively keeping thought steps accessible to subsequent steps \emph{during training} lets the model bypass memory tokens by retrieving information directly from these steps, leaving the model's ability to compress and retrieve information through memory tokens insufficiently trained. We therefore introduce a hybrid training scheme, in which only some thought steps are directly accessible through attention to subsequent steps, while the other thought steps are masked, forcing the model to use memory tokens for compression and retrieval. Across 4 reasoning benchmarks, HybridThinker matches the uncompressed baseline, advancing the state of the art in CoT compression by 5.8 points on average accuracy with similar inference time. Ablation studies confirm that both temporary thought-step retention and the hybrid training scheme contribute to these gains.

</details>

### [148] [Human-in-the-Loop Contextual Bandits for Short-Term Rental Dynamic Pricing: Structural Equivalence of Historical Warm-Up and Approval-Gated Live Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02595)
*Oleg Miroshnichenko*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出HITL-GB框架，通过人类审批约束下的历史数据实现带状推荐的快速冷启动，将初始学习周期从约150次压缩至30次，在短租市场中显著提升动态定价效率，并证明该方法在医疗、信贷等高风险领域具有通用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 短租市场动态定价面临高财务风险、需可解释性及反馈稀疏（每晚仅一次预订）的挑战，纯在线学习算法因长冷启动期而难以实用。人类审批虽为约束，但可转化为统计优势。

Method: 引入人类在环路门控强化学习框架（HITL-GB），利用历史数据（来自确定性策略）作为先验信息，通过正则化岭回归进行后验初始化，实现对上下文贝叶斯算法的有效暖启动。

Result: 在真实短租数据上验证，使用HF-TS类算法时，有效冷启动期由~150次减少至~30次；结构等价性结果适用于医疗、信贷、内容审核等需人类审批的高风险领域。

Conclusion: 人类审批并非部署障碍，而是可被利用的统计资源，在受监管领域中能显著加速学习过程并保障安全性。

Abstract: Dynamic pricing in short-term rental (STR) markets presents a distinctive challenge for online learning algorithms: pricing decisions carry significant financial risk, operators require explainability, and market feedback is sparse (one booking outcome per listed night). We introduce the Human-in-the-Loop Gated Bandit (HITL-GB) framework, in which a contextual bandit algorithm generates price recommendations but a human agent retains authority to accept, modify, or reject each recommendation before it is applied. We show that under this approval constraint, historical pricing data -- collected under a prior deterministic policy -- is structurally equivalent to on-policy warm-up data for initialising the bandit's posterior, bypassing the weeks-to-months cold-start period that renders pure online bandit learning impractical in sparse-feedback markets. We formalise the approval-gated reward signal, derive a regularised ridge-regression warm-up procedure from historical episodes, and validate the approach on real STR production data (anonymised urban market, 2 rooms, April 2022 -- April 2026, 1,461 nightly pricing episodes). Our warm-up procedure compresses effective cold-start from ~150 episodes to ~30 episodes when initialising agents from the Hierarchical Factored Thompson Sampling (HF-TS) family. We further argue that the structural equivalence result is domain-agnostic: any high-stakes domain where human approval is legally or operationally required -- including clinical drug dosing, credit origination, content moderation, and radiological diagnosis -- satisfies the same conditions and benefits from the same warm-up strategy. In regulated industries, mandatory human oversight is thus a statistical asset rather than a deployment constraint.

</details>


### [149] [Spectral Asymptotics of Neural Network Loss Landscapes: An Exact Decomposition of the Curvature Exponent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02596)
*Anherutowa Calvo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了Hessian特征值与梯度奇异值之间幂律关系中的曲率指数α在不同层类型中系统性变化的原因。通过提出谱对齐分解公式α = 2 + d logΦ_k / d logσ_k，将问题转化为几何层面的对齐性分析，并在LayerNorm、残差连接和softmax头等结构上验证。该分解导出一个无自由参数的谱传输恒等式s = αγ，可在93个层、5种架构、3个数据集上以~2%中位误差准确预测Hessian衰减指数。进一步证明曲率集中在每层约一个有效方向，并提出自适应预条件器T(σ;α)，基于梯度奇异基的Spectral Newton方法在视觉任务中优于AdamW。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解深度神经网络中曲率指数α为何在不同层类型（如卷积、Transformer注意力、MLP投影）中呈现系统性差异，从而揭示其背后的几何机制并建立可泛化的理论框架。

Method: 提出谱对齐分解公式，通过分析克罗内克因子特征基与梯度奇异方向之间的对齐度Φ_k，推导出α与几何结构的关系；利用高阶向量乘积（HVP）和奇异值分解（SVD）独立估计α和γ，验证谱传输恒等式；结合泽塔函数边界分析参与度，证明曲率集中性；设计架构自适应预条件器T(σ;α)并实现Spectral Newton优化器。

Result: 谱对齐分解成功解释α的层间差异；谱传输恒等式在多种架构与数据集上实现~2%中位误差的s预测；曲率集中在单个有效方向；Spectral Newton在视觉任务中超越AdamW。

Conclusion: 曲率指数α的变化源于网络结构引起的谱对齐特性，其背后存在普适的几何规律。通过谱传输恒等式和自适应预条件器，可构建更高效的优化算法，为理解深层网络优化动态提供新视角。

Abstract: The curvature exponent $α$ in $h_k \propto σ_k^α$ -- governing how Hessian eigenvalues scale with gradient singular values -- varies systematically across layer types ($α\approx 2$ for convolutions, $\approx 1$ for transformer attention, $< 1$ for MLP up-projections). Why? We prove the Spectral Alignment Decomposition: $α= 2 + d\logΦ_k / d\logσ_k$, where $Φ_k$ measures alignment between Kronecker factor eigenbases and gradient singular directions. This reduces "why does $α$ vary?" to a geometric question we answer for LayerNorm, residual connections, and softmax heads. The decomposition implies a spectral transfer identity $s = αγ$ linking curvature exponent, effective gradient rank-decay $γ$, and Hessian decay exponent $s$. The identity is algebraic; its empirical content is that $α$ and $γ$, fit on independent data (HVPs vs. SVD), recover $s$ to ~2% median error across 93 layers, five architectures, and three datasets -- with no free parameters. A zeta-function bound on participation ratio shows curvature concentrates onto effectively one direction per layer. As a proof of concept, we derive the architecture-adaptive preconditioner $T(σ;α)$ and show that Spectral Newton -- implementing $T$ in the gradient singular basis -- outperforms AdamW on vision benchmarks where $α\approx 2$.

</details>


### [150] [Making Brain-Computer Interfaces More Secure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02597)
*Md Fahimul Kabir Chowdhury,Gahangir Hossain*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于EEG的脑机接口虽在分类准确率上取得进展，但对安全性和鲁棒性的关注不足。已有研究表明，这类系统易受微小且精心设计的对抗攻击影响，可能导致误诊，因此亟需评估并提升模型在对抗扰动下的稳定性，以确保其可靠部署。

Method: 提出一种轻量级自定义卷积神经网络（CNN）架构，用于建模和分析EEG信号在对抗攻击下的表现。采用梯度基对抗攻击场景，在两个公开EEG数据集上进行实验，并与EEGNet、DeepConvNet、SleepEEGNet等三种先进模型进行对比分析。

Result: 实验结果表明，所提出的轻量级CNN模型在多种对抗攻击下均表现出更高的分类准确率和更强的鲁棒性，优于对比的基准模型，说明该架构在对抗环境下具有更好的稳定性与实用性。

Conclusion: 轻量级自定义CNN架构可有效提升基于EEG的脑机接口系统在对抗攻击下的鲁棒性，为实现更安全可靠的脑机接口应用提供了可行路径。

Abstract: The development of brain-computer interfaces (BCIs) based on electroencephalograms (EEGs) has advanced significantly mainly to machine learning. Although the majority of earlier research has been on increasing classification accuracy, relatively little focus has been placed on security and robustness. According to recent research, EEG-based BCIs are susceptible to adversarial attacks, which can cause misdiagnosis due to minute, well-crafted disturbances. Evaluating model robustness against such perturbations is therefore critical for ensuring reliable deployment. In this study, we propose a lightweight custom Convolutional Neural Network (CNN) architecture to investigate adversarial robustness in EEG-based BCIs. The suggested method is assessed using two EEG datasets and contrasted with three novel CNN models tailored to EEG, namely EEGNet, DeepConvNet, and SleepEEGNet, under gradient-based adversarial attack scenarios. According to experimental findings, the suggested model continuously performs better in classification under adversarial perturbations compared to baseline models, indicating improved robustness. These findings highlight the potential of lightweight architectures for enhancing the reliability of EEG-based BCI systems under adversarial conditions.

### [151] [Assessing Region-Level EEG Contributions to Cognitive Workload Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02598)
*Jacob Wong,Sohan Singh,Prannaya Gupta,Jin Xing Ang,Kritika Johari,U-Xuan Tan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于头皮区域的EEG认知负荷估计评估框架，通过分析四个公开的EEG负荷数据集，发现额区和额中央区域的电极在不同任务、数据集和受试者间具有最稳定的预测能力，显著优于全头皮基线，且使用更少电极即可实现更高性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前EEG用于认知负荷评估时，各脑区电极贡献的一致性尚不明确，亟需一种可量化、通用的评估方法以支持高效、鲁棒的负荷监测系统设计。

Method: 采用模型无关、基于性能的评估策略，对四个公开数据集进行大规模分析，仅使用解剖学定义的头皮区域电极特征训练与评估模型，并在混合受试者与受试者独立两种协议下评估区域重要性，通过秩次聚合确保结果稳健性。

Result: 额区电极组在所有数据集和受试者独立评估中相对排名提升15-20%，表现优于全头皮基线；额中央区域预测性能最稳定，而后部及枕部区域贡献不一致。

Conclusion: 认知负荷相关的EEG信息主要集中在额区和额中央区域，建议在设计高效、通用的EEG负荷监测系统时优先考虑这些区域的电极布局。

Abstract: Accurate and generalizable estimation of cognitive workload from electroencephalography (EEG) is critical for human-centered and safety-critical systems. Although EEG is widely used for workload assessment, the consistency of region-level EEG contributions across tasks, datasets, and subjects remains unclear. This paper presents a region-level evaluation framework for EEG-based workload prediction in which models are trained and evaluated using features extracted exclusively from electrodes belonging to anatomically defined scalp regions. We perform a large-scale analysis across four publicly available EEG workload datasets spanning diverse task demands, recording hardware, and electrode montages. Region importance is quantified using a model-agnostic, performance-based approach under both mixed-subject and subject-independent evaluation protocols, with results aggregated using a rank-based strategy to ensure robustness across experimental configurations. Across all datasets and subject-independent evaluations, frontal electrode groups outperform the full-scalp baseline by approximately 15-20% in relative rank position while using substantially fewer electrodes. Fronto-central regions exhibit the most stable predictive utility, whereas posterior and occipital regions contribute less consistently across experimental conditions. These findings indicate that workload-relevant EEG information is most consistently retained within frontal and fronto-central electrode groups, supporting the design of efficient and generalizable EEG-based workload monitoring systems.

### [152] [Testing the Test: Score-Direction Instability in Class-Split Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02601)
*Alejandro Ascarate,Leo Lebrat,Rodrigo Santa Cruz,Clinton Fookes,Olivier Salvado*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出，现有的类分割异常检测评估协议在异常类与正常类在表示空间中重叠时可能失效，导致异常得分退化甚至反转；提出一种无需训练的诊断方法‘邻域类别泄漏’，可有效预测得分方向的不稳定性，并在多个数据集和空间中验证其有效性，建议将此类基准视为几何依赖性的压力测试而非无条件的异常检测能力证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有类分割评估协议在异常类与正常类在表示空间重叠时可能导致异常得分不可靠，缺乏对评估方法局限性的认识，亟需一种简单有效的诊断工具来识别此类问题。

Method: 提出‘邻域类别泄漏’作为训练-free诊断方法，通过分析正常类样本邻域中是否存在异常类样本，判断异常得分方向是否稳定。

Result: 在Fashion-MNIST、CIFAR-10和Imagenette数据集上，无论在像素空间还是VAE潜在空间，该方法均能准确预测异常得分方向的不稳定性，表明当前评估协议存在几何依赖性缺陷。

Conclusion: 类分割异常检测基准应被视为几何依赖性的压力测试，而非无条件证明模型具备异常检测能力的可靠依据。

Abstract: Within-dataset class-split evaluation is widely used as a proxy for fully unconditional out-of-distribution anomaly detection. We show that this protocol can become ill-posed when the held-out anomaly class overlaps the normal mixture in representation space. In this regime, anomaly scores may collapse toward chance or even invert, and the preferred score direction can depend on the unknown anomaly class. We introduce a simple training-free diagnostic, neighborhood class leakage, and show that it predicts score-direction instability across Fashion-MNIST, CIFAR-10, and Imagenette, in both pixel and VAE latent spaces. Our results suggest that class-split AD benchmarks should be treated as geometry-dependent stress tests rather than unconditional evidence of anomaly-detection ability.

</details>


### [153] [Graph Mamba Survival Analysis Based on Topology-Aware ordering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02602)
*Yuanfang Chen,Peiqiang Yan,Yuntao Shou,Qian Zhao,Xiangyong Cao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于拓扑感知排序的图Mamba生存分析框架（TopoMamSurv），以解决全切片图像（WSIs）生存分析中Transformer计算复杂度高、Mamba对输入顺序敏感及单向建模限制等问题。通过拓扑感知排序（TAO）提升节点顺序的合理性，结合双向Mamba模块与GCN，实现局部聚合与全局捕捉的分层特征学习，有效平衡长程依赖建模、计算效率与空间结构利用，在五个TCGA数据集上验证了其综合性能优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在计算病理学中，全切片图像（WSIs）的生存分析对患者预后评估至关重要，但面临计算复杂度高、长程依赖建模困难以及空间结构利用不足等挑战。现有Transformer模型因$O(N^2)$时间复杂度难以处理大规模WSIs图结构；而Mamba虽具备线性复杂度优势，却对输入顺序敏感，传统节点排序方法未能充分考虑图的拓扑连通性，且其单向架构无法捕捉图像的双向空间结构，限制了建模效果。

Method: 提出拓扑感知排序（TAO）策略，优化节点输入顺序以适应Mamba对序列敏感性的需求；设计双向Mamba模块，增强对图像双向空间结构的建模能力；融合图卷积网络（GCN），构建‘局部聚合-全局捕捉’的分层特征学习架构，实现高效且结构感知的特征提取。

Result: 在五个TCGA数据集上的实验表明，该框架在生存分析任务中显著优于对比方法，展现出更强的预测性能和鲁棒性；可视化结果证实TAO策略提取的节点具有更高相似性，验证了排序策略的有效性。

Conclusion: TopoMamSurv框架通过拓扑感知排序、双向语义建模与层次化特征融合，系统性地解决了大尺度WSIs生存分析中的计算效率与结构建模矛盾，为计算病理学中的长程依赖建模提供了高效且精准的新范式。

Abstract: In computational pathology, Whole Slide Images (WSIs) survival analysis is crucial for patient prognosis assessment, but it faces multiple technical challenges. Although the Transformer captures long-range dependencies through its self-attention mechanism, its $O(N^2)$ time complexity causes a severe computational bottleneck in large-scale WSIs graph structures. The Mamba model breaks through the Transformer's computational bottleneck with linear complexity. But, owing to Mamba's high sensitivity to the order of input data, traditional node sorting methods in Graph Mamba, such as those based on node degree or subgraph size, fail to adequately account for the topological connectivity of graph data. This inadequacy consequently restricts the performance of Mamba's sequential modeling. Moreover, its unidirectional architecture cannot leverage the bidirectional spatial structure of images. To address these challenges, this paper proposes a novel Graph Mamba survival analysis framework based on topology-aware ordering (TopoMamSurv) to adapt to the sequential sensitivity of Mamba. Our visualization experiments further confirmed that the nodes extracted through the topology-aware ordering (TAO) strategy indeed exhibit higher similarity. Furthermore, we designed a bidirectional Mamba module and integrated a Graph Convolutional Network (GCN) to achieve bidirectional spatial context modeling of images, forming a hierarchical feature learning architecture for "local aggregation - global capture." This framework effectively reconciles the contradiction between long-range dependency modeling, computational efficiency, and spatial structure utilization in WSIs analysis through its systematic design of TAO, bidirectional semantic modeling, and hierarchical feature fusion. This framework has been validated for its comprehensive performance advantage on five TCGA datasets.

</details>

The methodology incorporates temporal drift analysis, SMOTE based rare event optimization, ensemble learning, provenance aware orchestration, and TreeSHAP based interpretability for governance inspection and audit reconstruction. We evaluate the framework against statistical classifiers, anomaly detection methods, temporal forecasting baselines, and a threshold based system using classification metrics (recall, F1, ROC AUC), calibration metrics (ECE, Brier score), and a governance oriented audit trace completeness metric measuring the fraction of flagged anomalies for which a deterministic source to escalation provenance chain can be reconstructed. Results are reported as mean and standard deviation across stratified five fold cross validation with paired significance testing. The framework reframes ESG reporting toward deterministic climate risk governance infrastructure supporting reproducibility, explainability, and operational auditability.

### [155] [Cross-Modal Contrastive Learning of ECG and Angiography Representations for Severe Stenosis Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02605)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Coronary artery stenosis is a common cardiovascular disease, with severe, untreated cases posing significant risks of heart attack. However, as no reliable stenosis-specific signal has been identified in ECGs, they can not currently be used for stenosis risk stratification. The obtained models successfully detect signals for stenosis diagnosis in ECGs and are the first to achieve high performance in severe stenosis classification. ### [156] [ReLoRA: Knowledge-Reusing Adaptation for Fast Rollout of Evolving LLM Services](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02606)
*Yang Xu,Zihuai Xu,Hongli Xu,Yunming Liao,Zhiwei Yao,Xitong Fu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ReLoRA 是一种高效的知识重用再适应框架，用于在大语言模型（LLM）持续演进时快速恢复服务可用的低秩适配器（LoRA），避免从头训练的高成本。它通过两步优化：1）基于贝叶斯优化的自适应LoRA初始化，融合旧适配器与基模型演化的信息以构建兼容性起点；2）带调度正则化的微调，先强正则快速收敛至高质量区域，再放松正则进行任务精调。实验表明，ReLoRA 可将服务就绪时间减少最多 8.9 倍，并提升准确率最高达 4.6%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当大型语言模型频繁更新时，原有的任务特定低秩适配器（LoRA）可能因与新基模型不兼容而失效。若每次更新都重新训练所有适配器，计算开销巨大且延迟服务部署；而直接使用旧适配器又会导致性能下降。因此需要一种高效、可复用的方法来快速恢复适配器性能。

Method: ReLoRA 包含两个核心步骤：(1) 自适应 LoRA 初始化，利用贝叶斯优化融合旧适配器与基模型演化信息，生成兼容性更强的初始参数；(2) 带调度正则化的微调策略，初期施加强正则以快速引导至高质量区域，后期放松正则以实现任务特异性优化。

Result: 在多个下游任务上，ReLoRA 显著缩短了服务就绪时间，最多减少 8.9 倍；同时在准确率上提升最高达 4.6%，优于现有基线方法。

Conclusion: ReLoRA 有效解决了持续演进的大语言模型中 LoRA 适配器的再适应难题，实现了高性能与低开销的平衡，为大规模模型服务的动态部署提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as continuously evolving services, where frequent base-model updates may invalidate previously deployed task-specific Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) adapters. For service providers managing numerous downstream model services, retraining each LoRA adapter from scratch for every updated base model is computationally prohibitive and delays service rollout. Meanwhile, the simpler alternative, i.e., naively applying the original LoRA adapter to the updated base model, often leads to degraded service quality due to adapter-backbone incompatibility. To address this problem, we propose ReLoRA, a knowledge-reusing re-adaptation framework that efficiently restores service-ready LoRA adapters for evolving LLM services while preserving or improving task performance. Specifically, ReLoRA comprises two key optimization steps: 1) Adaptive LoRA initialization leverages Bayesian optimization to construct a compatibility-aware starting point by fusing information from both the previously deployed task adapter and the base model's evolution; 2) Fine-tuning with scheduled regularization first rapidly steers the adapter to a high-quality region via strong regularization, followed by relaxed regularization for task-specific refinement. This design enables rapid service-quality recovery with reduced re-adaptation overhead. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ReLoRA reduces time-to-readiness by up to 8.9$\times$ and improves accuracy by up to 4.6\% compared to baselines.

</details>


### [157] [Geometry-Aware Tabular Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02607)
*David Turtora Zagardo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Geometry-Aware Tabular Diffusion (GATD)，通过显式引入列间值差的夹角和长度作为输入与辅助目标，增强表格扩散模型的去噪器，实现更优的隐私保护数据合成。该方法在10个数据集上表现优异，性能超越现有基准，且参数量减少3.5倍（分类任务最多减少25倍），同时可迁移至GNN和Transformer架构，验证了显式关系监督作为通用归纳偏置的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散模型依赖隐式机制捕捉表格数据中列间的复杂关系，缺乏对列间结构信息的显式建模，导致生成质量受限。为提升表格数据合成的质量与效率，需引入更有效的结构感知机制。

Method: GATD通过计算列值差异的成对夹角与长度，并将其作为额外输入与辅助损失目标注入扩散去噪过程；采用MLP架构实现高效建模，并支持扩展至GNN与Transformer等不同架构。

Result: 在10个数据集上，GATD在Shape、Trend和下游任务（F1/RMSE）分别取得8/10、7/10、9/10的领先表现，相比基线降低27%的Shape误差和20%的Trend误差；参数量平均减少3.5倍，分类任务最高减少25倍；默认损失权重可有效迁移至其他架构，在27/30和25/30的组合中提升Shape与Trend性能。

Conclusion: 显式的关系监督（即基于几何特征的结构信息）是提升表格扩散模型性能的高效且可迁移的归纳偏置，GATD实现了更高效率与更优生成质量，为隐私保护的数据合成提供了新范式。

Abstract: Tabular synthesis is critical for privacy-preserving sharing and augmentation, yet diffusion models rely on implicit mechanisms to capture inter-column relationships. We introduce Geometry-Aware Tabular Diffusion (GATD), which augments tabular diffusion denoisers with pairwise angles and lengths computed from column value differences and used as inputs and auxiliary targets. Our MLP instantiation achieves state-of-the-art benchmark performance while using 3.5x fewer parameters on average (up to 25x for classification tasks): on ten datasets, it wins 8/10 Shape, 7/10 Trend, and 9/10 downstream utility (F1/RMSE), reducing Shape and Trend error by 27% and 20%. Default loss weights transfer to GNN and Transformer denoisers, improving Shape on 27/30 and Trend on 25/30 architecture-dataset cells. A matched ablation shows supervision (not extra inputs or capacity) drives the gain. This shows explicit relational supervision is a portable inductive bias for tabular diffusion.

### [158] [Pruning Deep Neural Networks via the Marchenko--Pastur Distribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02608)
*Leonid Berlyand,Theo Bourdais,Houman Owhad,Yitzchak Shmalo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于Marchenko-Pastur随机矩阵理论的深度神经网络剪枝方法，可在极小微调预算下保持模型精度。核心贡献在于短周期校准与微调即可实现高精度保留，避免长期重训练。理论提供确定性数据路径证书：若移除组件的对数效应较小，则剪枝可降低弹性网络目标函数，并保护稀疏裕度超过扰动两倍的样本。零预算剪枝可达完美效果；剪枝-恢复扩展模型在固定稀疏执行模式中模拟权重恢复；带L2正则化的模型显示随机成分随训练消失，而显著峰值稳定存在。在独立同分布高斯条件下，拟合的MP边缘σ+可作为层间剪枝预算的高概率信号。在ImageNet-1k上，仅经三轮蒸馏后，ViT-B/16 2:4+ToMe达到83.41%准确率（仅比全连接低1.70个百分点），同时实现59.81%的稀疏执行计算量减少，并获得1.388倍A40原生2:4后端加速；无ToMe的A100端点达2.705倍加速。结构化稀疏下，ViT-B/16 6:12达83.74%，ViT-L/16 8:16达85.33%（仅低0.51个百分点），ConvNeXtV2-Base 12:16达86.35%（仅低0.37个百分点）。对于CNN，ResNet50 8:16达75.87%（仅低0.26个百分点），ResNet152d CAST-conv+permutation达81.33%（仅低1.53个百分点），计算量约减50%，且在A40 im2col+2:4稀疏GEMM审计下实现1.62倍加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有剪枝方法通常依赖较长的微调阶段以恢复精度，但实际部署场景中微调资源有限。本文旨在开发一种在极小微调预算下仍能保持高精度的剪枝方法，提升模型压缩的实际可用性。

Method: 基于Marchenko-Pastur随机矩阵理论，构建剪枝的理论框架，通过分析移除组件的对数效应来判断剪枝影响。引入零预算剪枝、剪枝-恢复扩展、L2正则化模型等机制，结合层间预算信号估计，实现高效剪枝与推理加速。

Result: 在ImageNet-1k上，多种模型在极小微调条件下实现高精度保留，同时大幅降低计算量，获得显著推理加速。例如，ViT-B/16 2:4+ToMe在仅三轮蒸馏后即达83.41%准确率，计算量减少近60%，加速比达1.388倍以上。结构化稀疏下，多个模型接近或超过原始精度，且加速比普遍超过1.5倍。

Conclusion: 该方法通过理论驱动的剪枝策略，在极小微调预算下实现了高性能与高效率的平衡，为实际部署中的模型压缩提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: We study a Marchenko--Pastur (MP) random-matrix approach to pruning deep neural networks with very small post-pruning fine-tuning budgets. The main practical contribution is accuracy retention under short calibration and fine-tuning schedules, rather than a long post-pruning reoptimization pipeline. The theory gives deterministic data-path certificates: if the removed component $R$ has small propagated logit effect $L_s \| R ψ_1(s) \|_\infty$, pruning decreases an elastic-net objective and preserves samples whose dense margin exceeds twice the perturbation. The zero-budget case gives perfect pruning; a prune--restore extension models weight restoration inside a fixed sparse-execution pattern; and an additive $L_2$-regularized model shows admissible random-like components vanish at the training limit, with persistent spikes stabilizing as the MP bulk collapses. Under iid-Gaussian sufficient conditions, the fitted MP edge $σ_+$ gives a high-probability layerwise budget signal.
  On ImageNet-1k, after only three distillation epochs, ViT-B/16 $2{:}4{+}$ToMe reaches $83.41\%$ top-1 ($-1.70$ pp from dense) at $59.81\%$ sparse-execution MAC reduction, with $1.388\times$ best-observed A40 native-$2{:}4$ backend speedup for the same checkpoint and ToMe graph; a separate no-ToMe A100 endpoint gives $2.705\times$. At structured sparsity, ViT-B/16 $6{:}12$ reaches $83.74\%$, ViT-L/16 $8{:}16$ dense+permutation reaches $85.33\%$ ($-0.51$ pp), and ConvNeXtV2-Base $12{:}16$ reaches $86.35\%$ ($-0.37$ pp). For CNNs, ResNet50 $8{:}16$ dense+permutation reaches $75.87\%$ ($-0.26$ pp), and ResNet152d CAST-conv+permutation reaches $81.33\%$ ($-1.53$ pp) at ${\sim}50\%$ MAC accounting with a $1.62\times$ A40 im2col$+2{:}4$ sparse-GEMM audit.

</details>

The capability improvements are marginal, but quality of life improvements are quite substantial. ### [160] [Hallucination Is Linearly Decodable from Mid-Layer Hidden States in Quantized LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02628)
*Aizierjiang Aiersilan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了开源大语言模型（LLM）的隐藏状态中是否存在线性可分的真实性信号，并确定该信号在哪个网络深度最强。在三个7B-8B指令微调模型（Llama-3.1-8B、Mistral-7B、Qwen2.5-7B）上，使用4位NF4量化加载，通过四个幻觉基准测试（TruthfulQA、HaluEval-QA、FEVER和一个受控合成集）提取每层隐藏状态，比较了四种检测方法：线性探针、MLP探针、INSIDE EigenScore、自一致性与注意力熵。结果显示，单个中间层的线性探针在保留分割上达到0.904–1.000的AUROC，而基于采样的检测器在同一协议下未超过0.541的AUROC。真实性信号近似线性，MLP探针仅比线性探针高出不超过0.01的AUROC。峰值探测层在自然语言基准测试中表现出一致的范围——对Llama和Mistral为第13–18层（共32层），对Qwen为第19–25层（共28层）。首层注意力熵在知识依赖场景中提供互补信号（在HaluEval-QA上达到0.866–0.941的AUROC），且无需额外推理成本。采样方法的低区分能力反映其与成对标签评估之间的结构性不匹配，而非方法本身的固有局限。代码与数据已发布，可在单张8GB GPU上完全复现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究开源大语言模型中是否存在可被线性探测的真实信号，以理解模型内部表征机制并提升幻觉检测能力，同时揭示不同检测方法的有效性差异及其内在原因。

Method: 在三种7B-8B指令微调模型上，使用4位NF4量化加载模型，提取各层隐藏状态；在四个幻觉基准测试上应用线性探针、MLP探针、INSIDE EigenScore、自一致性及注意力熵等四种检测方法；通过在保留分割上的性能评估，分析真实性信号的位置与强度。

Result: 线性探针在单个中间层即可实现0.904–1.000的AUROC，显著优于其他方法；峰值探测层集中在模型中段（如第13–18层或第19–25层）；注意力熵在知识依赖任务中表现优异；采样方法表现差源于结构不匹配而非方法本身缺陷。

Conclusion: 开源大语言模型的隐藏状态中存在强线性真实性信号，其最佳探测位置集中在中层，且可通过简单高效的方法（如线性探针或首层注意力熵）有效检测，为幻觉识别提供了新路径。

Abstract: We investigate whether open-source LLMs encode a linearly separable truthfulness signal in their hidden states, and at which network depth this signal is strongest. Across three $7$B--$8$B instruction-tuned models (Llama-3.1-8B, Mistral-7B, Qwen2.5-7B) loaded in $4$-bit NF4 quantization, we extract per-layer hidden states on four hallucination benchmarks (TruthfulQA, HaluEval-QA, FEVER, and a controlled synthetic set) and compare four detection approaches: linear and MLP probes, INSIDE EigenScore, self-consistency, and attention entropy. A linear probe on a single mid-network layer achieves $0.904$--$1.000$ AUROC on held-out splits, while sampling-based detectors do not exceed $0.541$ AUROC under the same protocol. The truthfulness signal is approximately linear: MLP probes rarely surpass linear probes by more than $0.01$ AUROC. Peak probing layers fall in a consistent band across model families on natural-language benchmarks -- blocks~$13$--$18$ of~$32$ for Llama and Mistral, and blocks~$19$--$25$ of~$28$ for Qwen. First-block attention entropy provides a complementary signal in knowledge-grounded settings ($0.866$--$0.941$ AUROC on HaluEval-QA) at no additional inference cost. The low discriminability of sampling methods under this protocol reflects a structural mismatch between paired-label evaluation and the information these methods access, rather than an inherent limitation of those methods. Code and data are released for full reproducibility on a single $8$\,GB GPU.

</details>


### [161] [Regime-Arrival Uncertainty in Generalization Bounds under Distribution Shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02657)
*Prince Poudel*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种新的框架，用于在马尔可夫切换分布下量化因制度组成不匹配带来的额外风险，实现了制度错配与制度敏感性的精确分解，并将泛化界扩展到β-混合数据，利用考虑谱间隙的有效样本量修正。研究还给出了合成数据和25年全球股权指数的极小极大下界。所提出的惩罚项是事后实现的泛化差距，而仅基于训练数据的估计器未表现出显著相关性：特征几何能检测危机，但无法捕捉时间到达模式。因此，该框架并非预测工具，未来制度组成的预测在罕见制度转换情况下仍为开放问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准泛化边界假设训练与部署分布相同或静态，未考虑制度切换环境中平静与危机状态比例不同的情况。实际应用中，分布可能随时间动态变化，尤其在金融等复杂系统中，需更精准地衡量模型在不同制度下的泛化性能。

Method: 提出一种针对马尔可夫切换分布的泛化分析框架，通过数学分解分离制度错配与制度敏感性；引入有效样本量修正（考虑谱间隙）以处理非独立同分布的β-混合数据；构造极小极大下界验证理论有效性；使用事后实现的泛化差距作为惩罚项，评估模型在制度不匹配下的表现。

Result: 成功实现制度错配与制度敏感性的精确分解；在合成数据和真实全球股权指数数据上验证了理论界限的有效性；证明了仅依赖训练数据的估计器对制度组成变化不敏感，而新框架能有效捕捉制度不匹配的影响。

Conclusion: 该框架为制度切换环境下的模型泛化提供了理论支持，强调了制度组成差异的重要性，但并未解决未来制度组成的预测问题，指出其仍是开放挑战。

Abstract: The standard generalization bounds assume that the training and deployment distributions are the same, or are static, and don't consider regime switching environments where the ratio of calm vs crisis states is different. This paper proposes a framework that generalizes regime-aware models by quantifying the extra risk due to regime composition mismatch, when distribution shifts are Markov-switching. We obtain an exact decomposition, separating regime mismatch from regime sensitivity; we extend the bound to beta-mixing data using the effective sample size corrected for the spectral gap; and we show a minimax lower bound for synthetic data and on 25 years of global equity indices. The proposed penalty is an ex post realized generalization gap, whereas the training-only estimator does not show significant correlation: the feature geometry of crises can be detected, but not the temporal arrival. Thus, the framework is not a forecast machine. Forecasting the composition of the future regime is an open question in the rare cases of regime change.

</details>

Abstract: Machine learning has accelerated quantum chemistry but is hindered by the prohibitive cost of generating high fidelity training data. ### [165] [Anomalies in Multivariate Time Series Benchmarks Are Mostly Univariate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02670)
*Marc Pinet,Julien Cumin,Samuel Berlemont,Dominique Vaufreydaz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究通过一个分段诊断框架评估了多变量时间序列异常检测（MT-SAD）模型中跨通道建模假设的有效性。结果显示，大多数真实数据中的异常都伴随着单变量通道的偏离，而非跨通道相关结构的变化。在合成数据中，仅当跨通道结构被破坏而单变量分布保持不变时，框架才能正确识别出纯跨通道异常。实验表明，当前主流基准数据集无法有效验证跨通道建模能力，且现有先进模型中跨通道建模并未带来显著性能提升。研究呼吁构建更具结构性多样性的评估数据集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多变量时间序列异常检测模型普遍依赖跨通道建模，但其有效性缺乏充分验证；尤其在真实数据中，异常是否真正源于跨通道结构变化尚不明确，亟需系统性评估机制以判断跨通道建模的必要性。

Method: 提出一种基于分段的诊断框架，用于分析每个标注异常段中是否存在单变量偏离、跨通道相关性变化或两者兼有；通过合成数据验证框架对纯跨通道异常的识别能力，并对比通道依赖（CD）与通道独立（CI）模型在真实和合成数据上的表现。

Result: 在八组公开基准上，绝大多数异常段均伴随单变量偏离，且跨通道结构变化极少独立出现；合成数据中框架能准确识别跨通道异常；实际模型对比显示，跨通道建模未带来明显性能提升。

Conclusion: 现有MT-SAD基准数据集不足以评估跨通道建模能力，应开发更具结构性多样性的新数据集以推动该领域发展。

Abstract: Many recent multivariate time series anomaly detection (MT-SAD) models incorporate cross-channel modeling, under the implicit assumption that the structure of anomalies may be spread across multiple channels. We evaluate this assumption on eight widely used public benchmarks by introducing a per-segment diagnostic framework that flags, for each labeled anomaly, whether at least one channel deviates individually from its normal history, whether the cross-channel correlation structure changes, or both. The framework shows that no crosschannel rupture occurs without an accompanying univariate deviation across a range of reasonable thresholds. A complementary metric also reveals that on six of the eight benchmarks, at least half of the labeled anomaly segments deviate univariately on 79% to 100% of their timesteps, reaching 100% on three of these datasets. To verify that our framework captures cross-channel structure when present, we construct synthetic data of phase-shifted sinusoidal channels with shared noise. Each anomalous segment is altered through one of two channelwise corruptions that preserve the per-channel marginal distribution while breaking cross-channel structure, and our framework correctly characterizes these segments as cross-channel-only. On these data, channel-dependent (CD) models successfully exploit the cross-channel signal whereas channel-independent (CI) ones fail. The CI/CD comparison of a recent SOTA detector on real benchmarks further confirms that CD modeling brings no measurable gain. We conclude that current MTSAD benchmarks are unsuitable for validating cross-channel modeling capabilities, and we call for the development of more structurally diverse evaluation sets. The code for this study is publicly available.

We establish the utility of NDCG in survival analysis by proving that it translates to guarantees on the performance of allocation. On historical heart transplant data from the US, our method dramatically boosts the NDCG of baseline models by 50-100%, which translates to tens of thousands of additional life years gained annually when deployed for transplant allocation. We anticipate that our framework will find broader applications in decision making with predictions.

Abstract: Multimodal systems often benefit from combining information across language, sound, and visual streams, but this benefit is not guaranteed. A modality that is useful for one input may become distracting for another, and local feature responses within the same modality can disagree with evidence from other sources. This work investigates how to adjust multimodal representations before they are merged by a downstream predictor. We develop a compact calibration module that compares each modality with the others at the summary level, extracts cues of cross-source support and conflict, and converts these cues into instance-wise and dimension-wise modulation signals. ### [168] [Locality Does Not Imply Reachability: Boundary Repair in Block-Sparse Causal Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02680)
*Zhibo Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了序列局部性与注意力图可达性之间的不匹配问题，提出通过结构依赖集分析固定块因果注意力中的边界伪影。指出在仅使用相同固定块因果掩码的情况下，目标表示仅依赖于其所在块前缀的令牌，导致边界复制分离现象，使模型性能上限受限（如准确率上界为1/K，交叉熵下界为log K）。通过相位条件覆盖函数揭示可达性同时受源-目标距离和目标在块内偏移的影响，进而预测稀疏模式失效、修复有效性及滑动窗口注意力与边界修复不可互换的原因。提出边界桥接注意力作为构造性证据，在不增加参数的前提下，在块边界处添加辅助因果边以保留固定块路径。实验表明增益集中在与覆盖对齐的诊断中，且8K-token Qwen2.5-7B模型验证了该覆盖不兼容模式。贡献在于构建了一个基于理论的诊断框架，并提供相位条件覆盖分析与最小修复方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究固定块因果注意力中序列局部性与注意力图可达性之间的不匹配，揭示其导致的边界伪影及其对模型性能的限制，旨在理解并修复此类结构性缺陷。

Method: 通过结构依赖集形式化边界伪影；引入相位条件覆盖函数分析可达性；设计边界桥接注意力作为无需额外参数的修复机制；通过控制实验与外部验证模型进行实证检验。

Result: 实验显示增益集中在覆盖对齐的诊断中；8K token模型验证了覆盖不兼容模式；边界桥接注意力有效提升可达性而不增加参数；揭示了滑动窗口与边界修复不可互换的本质原因。

Conclusion: 本文建立了理论指导的诊断框架，揭示了块稀疏因果注意力中的局部性-可达性错配问题，提出了相位条件覆盖分析方法与最小修复方案——边界桥接注意力，为优化稀疏注意力架构提供了新视角。

Abstract: Sparse causal attention is usually described by sequence locality: nearby tokens should remain easy to access, while distant tokens may be dropped to reduce cost. This paper studies a mismatch between sequence locality and attention-graph reachability. In fixed block causal attention, two adjacent tokens can be disconnected in the attention graph at every depth. We formalize this boundary artifact through structural dependency sets: if every attention layer uses the same fixed block causal mask and all remaining operations are positionwise, a target representation can depend only on tokens in its own block prefix. This yields an architecture-level boundary-copy separation for a constructed K-way boundary-copy distribution, with top-1 accuracy upper bound 1/K and expected cross-entropy lower bound log K. We then derive phase-conditioned coverage functions showing that reachability depends on both source-target distance and the target's offset within its block. These coverage laws predict when a sparse pattern should fail, when a repair can help, and why sliding-window attention and boundary repair are not interchangeable. Boundary Bridge Attention is treated as a constructive witness: it preserves the fixed block path and adds zero-additional-parameter auxiliary causal edges near block boundaries using shared projections. Controlled 1024-token experiments show that gains concentrate in coverage-aligned diagnostics. As secondary external-validity evidence, a fixed-checkpoint 8K-token Qwen2.5-7B probe shows the same coverage-incomparability pattern. The contribution is a theory-guided diagnostic framework for locality-reachability mismatch in block-sparse causal attention, together with phase-conditioned coverage analysis and a minimal constructive repair.

</details>

Abstract: On-Policy distillation (OPD) in large language models is shifting from full-trace KL supervision toward more selective training paradigms. Recent OPD methods increasingly focus on selecting which trajectories to learn from, which tokens are most informative, and which supervision signals are most reliable. Motivated by this trend, we rethink optimization granularity of OPD and propose \fireicon\ FiRe-OPD (Filter, then Reweight), which jointly adjusts supervision signals at both trajectory and token levels. In details, FiRe-OPD first filters trajectories to remove low-quality rollout samples, and then applies soft reweighting within the retained trajectories to emphasize informative tokens. Compared with hard token selection, FiRe-OPD leverages a soft-weighting mechanism to effectively mitigate information loss and enhance optimization stability, thereby achieving finer-grained OPD optimization. We validate the effectiveness of FiRe-OPD across strong-to-weak, single-teacher, and multi-teacher settings, and demonstrate its superiority over recent token-level OPD methods ( (e.g., +6.25 on AIME 2024 in strong-to-weak, +18.81 on Miner in multi-teacher). Our code is available at https://github.com/YuYingLi0/FiRe-OPD.

Abstract: Knowledge of real-time road slipperiness, or even better, a refined estimate of peak grip potential, is a critical input for vehicle warning and intervention control systems. ### [172] [Representational Capacity: Geometric Limits on Feature Representation in Transformer Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02765)
*Alexander Guha*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了Transformer语言模型中模型维度$d_{model}$对特征表示几何极限的影响，基于线性表示与超位置假设，提出通过嵌入矩阵的余弦相似度分布来估计模型可支持的近正交方向数量。研究发现，不同模型存在高ε（缺乏近正交结构）与低ε（保持近正交结构）两类，并指出传统Johnson-Lindenstrauss引理低估了训练后表示的打包效率，提出基于向量数与维度比$k/d$的修正容量公式，显著降低预测误差。最终定义了表征容量为潜在空间中可区分方向的上界，其对ε呈指数敏感，且大模型更倾向于紧约束正交性而非最大化容量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索模型维度在设定特征表示几何极限中的作用，理解训练后表示如何有效利用隐空间，解决现有理论低估实际表示容量的问题。

Method: 1. 以嵌入矩阵作为近正交性约束的可测量代理；2. 通过分析成对余弦相似度分布确定模型允许的偏差ε；3. 应用并修正Johnson-Lindenstrauss引理，引入基于$k/d$的比例关系推导新容量公式；4. 在多个开源模型上验证分类与容量预测效果。

Result: 1. 模型可分为高ε（无近正交结构）和低ε（保持近正交结构）两类；2. 修正后的容量公式将预测误差降低两个数量级；3. 表征容量对ε呈指数敏感，大模型偏好更严格的正交性约束。

Conclusion: 模型维度不仅影响容量，还通过控制近正交性约束决定表征能力。大模型倾向于维持更紧密的正交结构，暗示可能存在稳定性-容量权衡、可用概念上限或规模混淆等机制，有待进一步研究。

Abstract: Model dimension ($d_{model}$) is a fundamental hyperparameter in transformer language models, yet its role in setting the geometric limits of feature representation remains under-explored. Grounded in the Linear Representation and Superposition Hypotheses - which propose that models encode features as near-orthogonal directions in latent space - we develop a framework for estimating how many such directions a model can support. We first establish the embedding matrix as a measurable proxy for near-orthogonality constraints across the latent space: the boundary between meaningful token relationships and incidental similarity in the pairwise cosine similarity distribution gives a concrete estimate of the model's accepted deviation $\varepsilon$ from perfect orthogonality. Applying this metric across dozens of open-source models reveals two classes: models with high $\varepsilon$ whose embeddings lack near-orthogonal structure, and models with low $\varepsilon$ that maintain it. We then show that the standard Johnson-Lindenstrauss lemma greatly underestimates the packing efficiency of trained representations, and derive an adjusted capacity formula in which the number of near-orthogonal directions depends on the ratio of vectors to dimensions ($k/d$) rather than the raw count - a single modification that cuts prediction error by two orders of magnitude with no extra parameters. Combining these results, we define representational capacity as an upper bound on the number of distinguishable directions available for features and embeddings in a model's latent space. Capacity is exponentially sensitive to $\varepsilon$, and larger models favor tighter orthogonality constraints over maximizing raw capacity - a pattern compatible with several explanations (a stability-capacity trade-off, a ceiling on usable concepts, or confounds with model scale) that we leave to future work.

### [173] [QUIVER: Quantum-Informed Views for Enhanced Representations in Large ML Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02785)
*Aritra Bal,Michael Binder,Markus Klute,Benedikt Maier,Michael Spannowsky*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: QUIVER introduces a quantum-informed feature view using quantum Fisher information to enhance classical machine learning models with geometric insights from variational quantum circuits. It improves performance on diverse datasets (QM9 and JetClass) without requiring fault-tolerant quantum hardware, offering a domain-agnostic method to integrate quantum geometry into standard models.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To enhance machine learning models with complementary, non-redundant features derived from quantum information theory, particularly by leveraging the intrinsic geometry of quantum state manifolds that classical methods struggle to capture.

Method: Train a variational quantum circuit (VQC) on the same task as the classical model, extract the quantum Fisher information matrix as a basis-independent summary of higher-order correlations, and fuse this quantum geometric feature into classical architectures via targeted modifications.

Result: QUIVER improves standard performance metrics on QM9 (molecule property prediction) and JetClass (jet flavor classification), demonstrating measurable gains even without fault-tolerant quantum hardware.

Conclusion: Quantum-geometric features extracted from simulated variational circuits can significantly enhance classical machine learning models, providing a practical, domain-agnostic pathway to leverage quantum-inspired representations in current AI systems.

Abstract: Large machine learning models benefit substantially from multimodal inputs that provide a complementary view of the same example. We introduce QUIVER (QUantum-Informed Views for Enhanced Representations, a paradigm that enriches classical data-driven features with a quantum Fisher view: a geometrically motivated, basis-independent summary of higher-order correlations captured by a variational quantum circuit (VQC) trained to perform the same task. Unlike classical feature augmentation, the quantum Fisher information matrix encodes the intrinsic geometry of the learned quantum state manifold. While this feature map, motivated by quantum information theory, is ordinarily non-trivial to model classically, it can surface statistical structure that additional classical data or model capacity finds difficult to learn. This makes the quantum Fisher view a genuinely complementary modality rather than a redundant one. We demonstrate that QUIVER improves standard performance metrics on two benchmark datasets from very different fields: QM9 for predicting molecule properties, and JetClass for predicting jet flavor at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC). The core contribution, however, is domain-agnostic: the quantum Fisher view can be fused into a broad class of model architectures via targeted modifications to the base architecture, to incorporate information about the quantum geometry of the problem. These results demonstrate that quantum-geometric features, extracted from simulated variational circuits, can deliver measurable value for standard machine learning tasks, well before the advent of fault-tolerant quantum hardware.

### [174] [Qift: Shift-Friendly No-Zero W2 Post-Training Quantization for Rotated W2A4/KV4 LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02823)
*Chi-Wei Huang,Chia-Chi Tsai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在哈达玛旋转量化流水线中两比特权重的标量层级集几何结构，发现标准W2层级集{-2,-1,0,+1}在激进的W2A4/KV4设置下易崩溃。通过分析预训练权重的零中心性与高斯化特性，提出Qift方法，采用固定非零层级集{+/-0.5, +/-1.5}或等效的{+/-1, +/-3}及幂次2变体{+/-1, +/-4}，实现无需训练、无学习码本、无分组网格、无零点的高效两比特量化。该方法在多个基准上优于传统方案，显著缩小与W3A4的差距，同时保持一半层为两比特精度，是一种简单、源感知且部署友好的混合精度替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准两比特量化（W2）在极端低精度设置（如W2A4/KV4）下性能下降严重，问题不仅源于位宽限制，更在于重建层级设计不合理；现有方法未能充分考虑权重分布的内在统计特性，亟需一种基于数据分布特性的新型固定层级集设计。

Method: 采用哈达玛旋转对权重进行预处理，使其分布近似零中心高斯；基于此统计模型，提出Qift方法，设计固定非零两比特层级集，避免依赖学习码本或零点；通过尺度不变比率分析确定最优内/外重心比范围（0.25–0.33），指导层级集选择。

Result: 在LLaMA-2-7B和LLaMA-3.1-8B模型上，Qift在纯W2A4困惑度、多层混合精度（如L=16）下的困惑度、下游任务准确率以及GPTQ残差行为方面均优于标准W2层级集；在保持半数层为两比特的同时，显著缩小与W3A4的性能差距，具备良好的部署适应性。

Conclusion: Qift通过揭示两比特权重的内在统计特性，提出一种无需训练、无需复杂设计的固定非零层级集方案，在保持极简架构的前提下实现了高性能低精度推理，为轻量级大模型部署提供了有效路径。

Abstract: Two-bit weight quantization is attractive for memory-efficient LLM inference, but the standard W2 level set {-2,-1,0,+1} often collapses under aggressive W2A4/KV4 settings. We study the scalar level-set geometry of two-bit weights in a Hadamard-rotated quantization pipeline. Conventional asymmetric W2 substantially improves over the standard level set, indicating that W2A4 failure is not only a bit-width problem but also a reconstruction-level problem. Across all 224 linear modules in each of LLaMA-2-7B and LLaMA-3.1-8B, pretrained weights are already nearly zero-centered, while Hadamard rotation primarily Gaussianizes their standardized shape: excess kurtosis and Q-Q error drop by orders of magnitude. Based on this approximate zero-centered Gaussian-like source model, we propose Qift, a fixed no-zero W2 level set for rotated W2A4/KV4 inference. The main level set is {+/-0.5, +/-1.5}, equivalently {+/-1, +/-3} under a half-scale reparameterization; a power-of-two variant uses {+/-1, +/-4} for sign-and-shift decoded weight application. Qift redesigns the fixed two-bit code-to-level mapping and is training-free, learned-codebook-free, group-grid-free, and zero-point-free, retaining the standard per-channel scale. A scale-invariant ratio analysis identifies an effective inner/outer centroid ratio range of 0.25 to 0.33, explaining why mirror no-zero (MNZ), Lloyd, NF2, and PoT-MNZ perform well while {+/-1, +/-2} does not. On both models, the no-zero level sets consistently improve pure W2A4 perplexity, L-layer mixed W2/W4 perplexity, downstream accuracy, and GPTQ residual behavior over the standard W2 level set. At L=16 mixed precision, they substantially narrow the gap to W3A4 while keeping half of the transformer layers at two-bit precision, giving a simple, source-aware, and deployment-friendly alternative to more complex learned W2 codebooks.

*Arda Fazla,Abolfazl Hashemi*

TL;DR: 本文提出一种两阶段样本评分函数，以解耦核心特征与虚假特征的学习动态，并分别评估其难度。该方法能够有效识别并优先选择包含因果相关特征的样本，即使在无群体标签的情况下也能提升模型性能。实验表明，使用所选样本训练的标准ERM模型在仅需10%原始数据的情况下，表现优于现有最先进的去偏技术。

Abstract: Real-world datasets often contain spurious correlations that are not causally related to the target label. When such correlations dominate the majority of training samples, models tend to rely on them, leading to misclassification of minority samples that do not exhibit the same spurious patterns. While a potential approach is to select subsets of data to better represent the minority samples, this may require access to group labels, which are typically unknown. Furthermore, as we demonstrate, widely used sample scoring functions in the invariant subset or coreset selection literature largely depend on spurious features and therefore fail to accurately capture the importance or difficulty of core, causally relevant features. Accordingly, we propose to mitigate spurious correlations by developing a two-stage sample scoring function that disentangles the learning dynamics of core and spurious features and evaluates their difficulty separately. Based on our proposed metric, we introduce a new algorithm to find and prioritize informative samples both with and without spurious correlations. Extensive experiments demonstrate that a standard ERM model trained on our selected samples achieves superior performance compared to state-of-the-art debiasing techniques, while requiring as little as 10\% of the original training data.

### [176] [Learning Coherent Representations: A Topological Approach to Interpretability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02841)
*Sigurd Gaukstad,Melvin Vaupel,Valdemar Kargård Olsen,Erik Hermansen,Benjamin Dunn*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为coherence的几何属性，用于增强深度神经网络中特征的可解释性。该属性受大脑神经编码机制启发，要求样本和特征在状态空间中形成连续的几何簇，并且每个样本由某些特征描述，每个特征也至少被一个样本需要。通过证明相干矩阵诱导了样本与特征之间具有有界交错的维托里斯-里普斯滤波，确保两者共享一致的拓扑结构。作者设计了一个可微的目标函数Coh，基于弗雷歇方差，用于训练过程中强制实现相干性。与仅限制激活数量的稀疏性不同，相干性关注的是激活的几何连通性，从而不仅产生可解释的特征，还生成可解释的特征空间。实验在自编码器（合成数据和旋转MNIST）及BERT的词嵌入中验证了该方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前深度神经网络中的特征往往缺乏可解释性，单个神经元可能对零散、无关的输入激活。为提升特征的可解释性，本文受生物神经编码（如网格细胞和头方向细胞）启发，提出一种新的几何约束——相干性，旨在使特征与样本在状态空间中形成连续的几何结构，从而增强模型的可解释性。

Method: 提出相干性概念，定义非负矩阵中行（样本）与列（特征）需在几何上形成簇状关联；利用维托里斯-里普斯滤波的有界交错性质证明其拓扑一致性；设计可微目标函数Coh，基于弗雷歇方差，用于在训练中优化相干性；应用于自编码器与BERT嵌入任务进行验证。

Result: 在合成数据、旋转MNIST和BERT语言数据上的实验表明，Coh能够有效引导模型学习出具有几何连续性的特征，显著提升特征的可解释性；同时保持良好的数据重构或表示性能，证明了相干性在实际应用中的有效性。

Conclusion: 相干性作为一种几何约束，能够有效提升深度神经网络中特征及其空间结构的可解释性。通过强制特征与样本在状态空间中形成几何连通的簇，Coh方法不仅使单个特征更具语义意义，还能构建整体可解释的特征空间，在多种任务中表现优异，为可解释人工智能提供了新思路。

Abstract: Deep neural networks learn representations where individual features often lack interpretable meaning; a single neuron may activate for scattered, unrelated inputs. We introduce coherence, a geometric property inspired by neural coding in the brain, where neurons like grid cells and head direction cells respond to contiguous regions of state space. A non-negative matrix is coherent if each row (sample) attends to geometrically clustered columns (features) and vice versa, and in addition every sample is well described by some feature and every feature is needed by some sample. We prove that coherent matrices induce a bounded interleaving between the Vietoris-Rips filtrations of samples and features, guaranteeing that both spaces share compatible topological structure. This geometric constraint facilitates interpretability. For example, if data lies on a circle, coherent features must tile that circle into contiguous arcs. We introduce Coh, a differentiable objective function based on Fréchet variance that enforces coherence during training. Unlike sparsity, which bounds how many samples a feature activates on, coherence bounds which samples, requiring geometric connectivity rather than only rarity. This yields not just interpretable features but an interpretable feature space. We validate Coh in an auto-encoder using synthetic and rotated MNIST datasets and in a token embedding of BERT using language data.

</details>


### [177] [Spectral-Progressive Thought Flow for Lightweight Multimodal Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02842)
*Yixian Shen,Zhiheng Yang,Qi Bi,Changshuo Wang,Shuai Wang,Jia-Hong Huang,George Floros,Prayag Tiwari,Anuj Pathania*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SpecFlow是一种轻量级多模态空间推理框架，通过将中间视觉思维表示在固定大小的离散余弦空间中，利用能量压缩特性保留全局布局和关系结构，并仅在需要更高空间精度时引入高频细节。通过无分类器引导，语言意图可引导视觉工作区的状态更新，而无需扩展上下文。该方法维持有界视觉工作区，其更新仅依赖于当前视觉状态和累积的文本轨迹，从而实现长时推理且延迟和内存使用稳定，不随推理深度增加。实验表明，SpecFlow在保持竞争力或更优推理性能的同时，计算量和KV缓存成本降低最多达2.1倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态空间推理通常依赖于长链的中间文本与视觉思维，导致视觉标记积累和密集跨模态注意力带来巨大的计算和内存开销。

Method: 提出Spectral-Progressive Thought Flow（SpecFlow），将中间视觉思维映射到固定大小的离散余弦空间，利用能量压缩保留全局结构；采用无分类器引导使文本思维引导视觉状态的流式更新，维持有界视觉工作区，仅依赖当前视觉状态与文本轨迹进行状态演化。

Result: SpecFlow在推理性能上达到或超过现有方法，同时将计算量和KV缓存成本减少最多2.1倍，支持长时推理且内存和延迟稳定。

Conclusion: SpecFlow通过高效视觉状态表示与语言引导的流式更新机制，实现了轻量化、高效率且可扩展的多模态空间推理，为长链条推理任务提供了可行解决方案。

Abstract: Multimodal spatial reasoning often relies on long chains of intermediate textual and visual thoughts, where accumulating visual tokens and dense cross-modal attention incur substantial computation and memory overhead. To address this challenge, we propose Spectral-Progressive Thought Flow (SpecFlow), a novel lightweight multimodal spatial reasoning framework that represents intermediate visual thoughts in a fixed-size discrete cosine space. By exploiting strong energy compaction, SpecFlow preserves global layout and relational structure while introducing high-frequency details only when increased spatial precision is required. To align visual state evolution with linguistic intent, classifier-free guidance enables autoregressive textual thoughts to steer flow-based updates of the visual workspace/state without expanding the context. As a result, SpecFlow maintains a bounded visual workspace whose updates depend only on the current visual state and accumulated textual trace, enabling long-horizon inference with stable latency and memory usage independent of reasoning depth. Empirical results show that SpecFlow achieves competitive or superior reasoning performance while reducing computation and KV cache costs by up to 2.1 times.

### [178] [A Systematic Evaluation of Current Architectures in Wind Power Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02849)

This study presents a systematic literature review focused on hybrid approaches to interval forecasting of wind generation, exploring the combination of deep learning, modal decomposition, and statistical methods. To guide the paper selection, Latent Dirichlet Allocation (LDA) was applied for topic modeling, enabling the identification of patterns and research trends. The findings emphasize that integrating hybrid models with decomposition techniques-such as Variational Mode Decomposition (VMD) and Ensemble Empirical Mode Decomposition (EEMD)-enhances forecast accuracy and reliability by narrowing prediction intervals without compromising coverage. Regarding interval construction, most studies adopt a dual-model strategy, independently forecasting the lower and upper bounds. Input data are commonly decomposed using techniques like EMD, EEMD, or VMD, which extract frequency-based components. These components serve as inputs to models such as LSTM or ELM, trained separately for each bound. This approach allows for targeted modeling of uncertainty, improving flexibility and precision, Interval quality is typically evaluated through metrics that balance coverage and interval width. The review also highlights challenges, including the lack of standardized evaluation metrics, computational complexity, and limited real-world validation. Overall, the study reinforces the value of interval forecasting for wind energy operations and offers insights for advancing model robustness and decision-making.

### [180] [GRZO: Group-Relative Zeroth-Order Optimization for Large Language Model Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02857)
*Liyan Tan,Yequan Zhao,Yifan Yang,Ruijie Zhang,Xinling Yu,Zheng Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GRZO是一种分组相对零阶优化器，通过每批次样本引入一个伪独立扰动，并利用分组相对归一化聚合每个样本的损失，将有效梯度方向数从1提升至批量大小，且无需额外前向计算开销，同时保持推理级内存效率。理论证明其方向无偏且方差随批量大小减小，收敛性优于MeZO。在RoBERTa-large、Llama3-8B和OPT-13B等多个任务上，GRZO相比MeZO平均提升3.0%准确率，且峰值GPU内存降低23%；作为MeZO核心的即插即用替代方案，显著提升稀疏、低秩及量化零阶变体平均性能达6.0%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决零阶优化在微调大语言模型时因梯度估计方差高而导致的部署限制问题。

Method: 提出GRZO优化器，每批次样本仅生成一个伪独立扰动，通过组相对归一化聚合各样本损失，从而将有效梯度方向数提升至批量大小，实现无额外前向开销的高效梯度估计。

Result: GRZO在多个模型和任务上表现优异：相比MeZO平均提升3.0%准确率，峰值GPU内存降低23%；作为MeZO核心的替代品，使稀疏、低秩及量化版本的零阶优化平均性能提升6.0%。

Conclusion: GRZO通过分组相对归一化机制，在不增加内存开销的前提下显著降低梯度估计方差，提升了零阶优化在大模型微调中的有效性与实用性，是现有方法的有效改进。

Abstract: Zeroth-order (ZO) optimization is a memory-efficient alternative to backpropagation for fine-tuning large language models, but its deployment is limited by the high variance of gradient estimation. We propose GRZO, a Group-Relative Zeroth-Order optimizer that draws one pseudo-independent perturbation per mini-batch example and aggregates the per-example losses through group-relative normalization, raising the effective gradient-direction count from one to the batch size at no additional forward cost while preserving inference-level memory. We prove that GRZO is directionally unbiased with variance shrinking proportionally to the batch size, yielding a tighter nonconvex convergence bound than MeZO. Across RoBERTa-large, Llama3-8B, and OPT-13B over multiple tasks, GRZO improves average accuracy on Llama3-8B by $+3.0$ over MeZO at $23\%$ lower peak GPU memory; as a drop-in replacement for the MeZO core, it lifts sparse, low-rank, and quantized ZO variants by $+6.0$ on average.
