### [181] [Forgetting is Not Erasure: Recovering Latent Knowledge via Transport Keys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02860)
*Archie Chaudhury*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文挑战了灾难性遗忘是表征问题的主流观点，指出大部分看似遗忘的现象实则源于内部阶段间接口漂移，而非任务相关计算的永久消失。通过一种缝合评估协议，将更新后网络的早期计算与前序网络的晚期计算结合，并引入紧凑的任务特定传输键来对齐接口。在ResNet风格网络和小型视觉变压器上，传输键能显著恢复任务A的性能，表明持续学习需要更好的机制来索引和重新访问潜在计算，而不仅仅是防止权重变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为灾难性遗忘是由于模型在连续学习过程中丢失了早期任务的特征表示。然而，本文质疑这一更强形式的观点，提出接口漂移可能是导致性能下降的主要原因，而非永久性记忆擦除。

Method: 提出一种缝合评估协议，将新模型的早期计算与旧模型的晚期计算进行组合，并引入任务特定的传输键作为接口对齐工具，通过少量配对锚点激活估计并验证其有效性。

Result: 在Split CIFAR-100数据集上，使用ResNet风格网络时，传输键几乎完全恢复了任务A的原始性能；在小型视觉变压器上也观察到类似恢复效果。

Conclusion: 持续学习的关键不在于防止权重变化，而在于建立更有效的机制来索引和重用已有的潜在计算，传输键作为一种接口对齐工具具有显著潜力。

Abstract: Catastrophic forgetting is often framed as a representational problem: after sequential training, a model appears to lose the features that supported performance on earlier tasks. We challenge the stronger form of this view. Across controlled continual-learning settings, we find that a significant portion of apparent forgetting can be attributed to interface drift between internal stages rather than permanent erasure of task-relevant computation. We study this phenomenon through a stitched evaluation protocol that combines early computation from a post-update network with late computation from its predecessor, optionally mediated by a compact, task-specific transport key. We describe transport keys at a systems level as compact interface-alignment operators estimated from a small set of paired anchor activations and evaluated through model stitching. On split CIFAR-100 with a ResNet-style network, transport keys recover most of the original Task A performance after sequential training on Task B. On a compact vision transformer, we observe a similar recovery pattern. These results suggest that continual learning may require better mechanisms for indexing and re-accessing latent computations, not only methods that prevent weight change.

### [182] [RRISE: Robust Radius Inference via a Surrogate Estimator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02876)
*Jong-Ik Park,Shreyas Chaudhari,Carlee Joe-Wong,José M. F. Moura*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RRISE 是一种新型的随机平滑框架，通过学习一个代理模型将认证过程压缩为单次前向传播，显著减少实时系统中的计算开销。它利用预计算的蒙特卡洛分类计数作为软标签进行训练，并通过一次性符合性校准生成可验证的保守认证半径，实现部署时可验证的鲁棒性保证。在多个图像分类基准上，RRISE 在保持高准确率的同时，将每查询的蒙特卡洛采样次数从高达 $10^4$ 次降至一次，仅需约 $10^5$ 次部署查询即可回收训练成本，在 CIFAR-100 和 Tiny ImageNet 上相比先前方法提升 1.23 到 1.91 倍的认证准确率，使随机平滑成为重复部署场景下实用的可证明鲁棒性路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机平滑依赖于每个输入的蒙特卡洛采样，导致实时系统中计算开销过大，但这种代价是结构性而非根本性的，可通过跨部署流共享信息来显著降低。

Method: 提出 RRISE 框架，训练一个代理模型以预测蒙特卡洛分类结果，使用软标签交叉熵损失；通过一次符合性校准将代理输出转化为保守的、可验证的认证半径。

Result: 在多个图像分类数据集上，RRISE 的认证准确率与固定预算蒙特卡洛方法相差不超过 0.84 个百分点，同时将每查询的基模型评估次数从最多 $10^4$ 次减少到一次；在 CIFAR-100 与 Tiny ImageNet 上认证准确率提升 1.23 到 1.91 倍，且可在约 $10^5$ 次部署后收回训练成本。

Conclusion: RRISE 实现了高效、可验证的随机平滑认证，使随机平滑在重复部署场景中具备实际可行性，为构建真实世界中的可证明鲁棒性系统提供了新路径。

Abstract: Randomized smoothing (RS) uses a smoothed classifier to provide architecture-agnostic certificates of $\ell_2$ classification robustness, but its dependence on per-input Monte Carlo (MC) sampling undermines its use in real-time systems. We argue that this cost is structural rather than fundamental, such that it can be significantly reduced by sharing information across the deployment stream. We introduce RRISE, an RS framework that compresses certification into a single forward pass through a learned surrogate. RRISE trains the surrogate against precomputed MC class-count targets via a soft-label cross-entropy loss and converts surrogate predictions into provably conservative certified radii through a one-time conformal calibration step. The resulting certificate is deployment-verifiable: whenever the calibrated radius is positive, the surrogate's prediction provably matches the smoothed classifier's and the smoothed classifier is constant on a ball of that radius around the input. Across image classification benchmarks, RRISE matches fixed-budget MC certified accuracy within $0.84$ percentage points while replacing up to $10^4$ noisy base-model evaluations per query with a single surrogate forward pass, recouping MC training cost after $\approx 10^5$ deployment queries. On CIFAR-100 and Tiny ImageNet, where the only prior offline-surrogate method collapses, RRISE achieves $1.23$ to $1.91\times$ higher certified accuracy, establishing efficient randomized smoothing as a practical path to certified robustness in repeated-deployment settings.

</details>


### [183] [Are we really tilting? The mechanics of reward guidance in flow and diffusion models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02884)
*Sanjit Dandapanthula,Nicholas M. Boffi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Reward guidance in diffusion models often causes reward hacking due to finite-particle approximation of the Doob h-function, even in simple settings. This leads to over-optimization of reward at the cost of fidelity and failure in selecting high-reward modes. The paper proposes a closed-form reward damping schedule to fix within-mode bias and clarifies the role of best-of-n sampling in mode selection. Experiments validate these insights across Gaussian mixtures, 2D checkerboard, and text-to-image generation.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Reward-guided diffusion models are powerful but suffer from reward hacking—over-optimizing reward while losing fidelity to the original distribution. Despite prior attributions to complex reward functions or training biases, the fundamental cause remains unclear. This work aims to identify the root cause in practical implementations.

Method: The authors analyze the finite-particle plug-in estimation of the Doob h-function in reward-guided diffusion, derive closed-form expressions for failure modes, propose a reward damping schedule to correct bias, and examine best-of-n sampling for mode selection.

Result: Closed-form analysis reveals two failure modes: reward hacking within each mode and inability to select high-reward modes. The proposed damping schedule eliminates within-mode bias without extra computation, and best-of-n sampling helps address mode selection issues. Experiments on synthetic and real-world tasks confirm theoretical findings.

Conclusion: Reward hacking in practical reward-guided diffusion stems from a fundamental approximation—the finite-particle plug-in estimator of the Doob h-function. Correcting this through a simple damping schedule and leveraging best-of-n sampling significantly improves performance and fidelity.

Abstract: Reward guidance algorithms steer a learned generative process toward the reward-tilted measure at inference time. While empirically powerful, these methods are prone to reward hacking: the guided model over-optimizes the reward at the cost of fidelity to the learned distribution. Prior work has attributed this to the complexity of neural reward functions or implicit biases in diffusion training, but its fundamental origins remain poorly understood. We show that reward hacking arises from an approximation made in most practical implementations of reward-guided diffusion -- finite-particle plug-in estimation of the Doob h-function -- even in the simplest non-trivial settings of Gaussian and Gaussian mixture targets with quadratic rewards. In closed form, we isolate two distinct failure modes of the plug-in estimator: it leads to reward hacking within each mode and it cannot select high-reward modes. We propose a closed-form reward damping schedule that corrects the within-mode bias with no additional compute, and clarify the role of best-of-n sampling in compensating for the mode selection failure. Experiments on Gaussian mixture targets, a 2D checkerboard, and FLUX.1 text-to-image generation confirm that our theoretical insights carry over to practical settings.

</details>


### [184] [Scalable Uncertainty Quantification for Extreme Weather Forecasting via Empirical Neural Tangent Kernels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02886)
*Jose Marie Antonio Miñoza,Rex Gregor Laylo,Sebastian C. Ibañez*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出基于神经正切核的不确定性量化（NTK-UQ）方法，利用最后一层的经验特征来估计深度学习天气模型的不确定性。理论分析表明，不确定性质量受模型架构影响，主要通过两种机制：一是方差坍缩机制，当特征空间的特征值截断秩接近有效秩时，高斯过程修正项会消耗几乎所有先验方差，导致热带气旋与常规条件无法区分；二是分解性能依赖极端天气的非高斯重尾结构，独立成分分析（ICA）通过高阶统计量（如峰度、负熵）可比奇异值分解（SVD）更有效地分离极端事件特征。基于特征谱集中度比率的数据驱动选择规则能正确判断四种架构中应使用ICA或SVD。相比传统的分割置信预测（split conformal prediction），NTK-UQ在90%覆盖率下预测区间更窄31–37%，且能自适应地随极端事件严重性调整区间大小，这是置信预测无法实现的。该框架无需重新训练，推理时仅需每样本一次矩阵-向量乘法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度学习天气模型虽在速度和精度上超越传统数值天气预报，但其确定性输出缺乏不确定性估计，这在极端天气事件中的高风险决策中构成关键缺陷。因此亟需一种高效、准确且无需重新训练的不确定性量化方法。

Method: 提出基于神经正切核的不确定性量化（NTK-UQ）方法，利用最后一层的经验特征。通过理论分析揭示不确定性质量受架构影响的两个机制：方差坍缩机制和基于高阶统计量的分解性能差异。采用数据驱动的选择规则决定使用ICA或SVD进行特征分解，并结合高斯过程修正项生成预测区间。

Result: NTK-UQ在90%覆盖率下相比分割置信预测显著缩小预测区间31–37%，并首次实现随极端事件严重性自适应调整的预测区间。该方法仅需单次矩阵-向量乘法即可完成推理时的不确定性计算，无需重训练。

Conclusion: NTK-UQ是一种高效、可扩展且架构敏感的不确定性量化框架，能够为深度学习天气模型提供自适应、精准的不确定性估计，适用于极端天气下的高风险决策支持。

Abstract: Deep learning weather models now match numerical weather prediction accuracy while running orders of magnitude faster, but produce deterministic forecasts without uncertainty estimates, a critical gap for high-stakes decisions during extreme weather events. This paper proposes Neural Tangent Kernel-based uncertainty quantification (NTK-UQ) using last-layer empirical features. Theoretical analysis predicts that UQ quality is architecture-dependent through two mechanisms. First, a variance collapse mechanism explains when UQ fails: when the eigenvalue truncation rank approaches the effective rank of the feature space, the GP correction term consumes nearly all prior variance, destroying discrimination between tropical cyclones and routine conditions; architectures with concentrated spectra (spectral operators) require aggressive truncation ($k \leq 10$), while attention-based models tolerate full-rank computation. Second, decomposition performance depends on the non-Gaussian, heavy-tailed structure of extreme weather: Independent Component Analysis exploits higher-order statistics (kurtosis, negentropy) to isolate heavy-tailed extreme-event features, achieving higher discrimination than singular value decomposition, which captures only second-order variance. A data-driven selection rule chooses ICA or SVD from the feature eigenspectrum concentration ratio, correctly prescribing the superior decomposition for all four evaluated architectures. Compared to split conformal prediction (the natural post-hoc baseline), NTK-UQ achieves 31--37\% sharper prediction intervals at 90\% coverage, and uniquely produces \emph{adaptive} intervals that scale with extreme event severity, which conformal prediction cannot achieve by construction. The framework requires no retraining; inference-time uncertainty requires only a single matrix-vector product per sample.

</details>


### [185] [A Nonmonotone Gradient-Based Algorithm for Symmetric Nonnegative Matrix Factorization and Graph Clustering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02887)
*Ryan Swart,Johannes Brust*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出SNMPBB，首个将非单调投影Barzilai-Borwein方法应用于对称非负矩阵分解（Symmetric NMF）的算法，显著提升了收敛速度。进一步扩展至图聚类（Graph-SNMPBB）和大规模低秩近似（LAI-SNMPBB），均证明全局收敛至一阶驻点，并保留了Barzilai-Borwein的曲率信息。实验显示，在合成数据上比SymANLS快6倍，真实世界聚类任务中性能相当或更优，且在34个SuiteSparse矩阵上优于现有最优方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统对称非负矩阵分解的投影梯度法收敛缓慢，限制了其在图聚类和机器学习中的应用。亟需更高效的优化方法以提升计算效率与适用性。

Method: 引入非单调投影Barzilai-Borwein方法构建SNMPBB，结合图拉普拉斯正则化与随机低秩近似，设计Graph-SNMPBB与LAI-SNMPBB，利用曲率信息加速迭代并保证收敛性。

Result: SNMPBB在合成数据上实现6倍速度提升；Graph-SNMPBB在六项真实聚类任务中达到或超越SymANLS精度；LAI-SNMPBB在34个SuiteSparse矩阵上优于当前最优方法，兼具更快运行时间和更优残差质量。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，基于投影梯度的算法在对称非负矩阵分解中具有强大潜力，通过引入非单调Barzilai-Borwein策略可显著提升效率与性能，为大规模图分析与聚类提供了高效新工具。

Abstract: Symmetric nonnegative matrix factorization (Symmetric NMF) approximates a matrix as $WW^T$ with nonnegative rectangular factor $W$. It has broad applications in graph clustering and machine learning. In contrast to the NMF, projected gradient methods for the symmetric problem had been associated with slow convergence. To address this, we introduce SNMPBB, the first adaptation of nonmonotone projected Barzilai-Borwein methods to Symmetric NMF, demonstrating that gradient algorithms are significantly more effective than previously understood. We further extend SNMPBB to graph clustering using the graph Laplacian regularization (Graph-SNMPBB) and to large problems with low-rank approximations (LAI-SNMPBB). For all variants we prove global convergence to first-order stationary points and also that Barzilai-Borwein curvature information is preserved with randomized approximations. On synthetic data, SNMPBB achieves 6 times speedup over the alternative SymANLS for similar residuals, with advantages growing at higher ranks. Across six real-world clustering benchmarks, Graph-SNMPBB matches or exceeds SymANLS accuracy. Lastly, LAI-SNMPBB outperforms state-of-the-art LAI-SymPGNCG on 34 SuiteSparse matrices in both runtime and residual quality.

We also benchmark performance against commonly used feature sets from prior breast cancer studies to assess the added value of multi-modal integration. Single-source and multi-modal inputs are evaluated across a range of machine learning models. ### [187] [Fast Unlearning at Scale via Margin Self-Correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02920)
*Federico Di Gennaro,Alexander Shevchenko,Fanny Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MArgin Self-Correction (MASC) is an efficient language-model unlearning method that uses an online stopping rule to avoid unnecessary computation and eliminate the need for downstream evaluation. It reduces the logit gap between the original next token and alternatives across token positions in forget sequences, stopping once the gap is sufficiently small. MASC achieves competitive forget-retain trade-offs at much lower computational cost than existing methods, with performance improving as model size increases.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing unlearning methods require extensive fine-tuning and checkpoint evaluation, leading to high computational costs and inefficiency. The goal is to reduce unnecessary training and eliminate the need for downstream validation during model selection.

Method: MASC actively minimizes the logit gap between the original next token and the most likely alternatives across token positions in forget sequences. It employs an online stopping criterion based on average gap reduction over a large proportion of positions, enabling early termination without relying on external evaluation.

Result: On TOFU, MUSE News, and MUSE Books datasets, MASC achieves strong forget-retain trade-offs with significantly lower computational cost compared to baselines. Performance improves with larger models: forget metrics remain stable while retention utility increases.

Conclusion: MASC provides an efficient, scalable unlearning solution by eliminating redundant training and avoiding post-training evaluation. Its online stopping rule enables faster, cost-effective unlearning, and its effectiveness grows with model scale.

Abstract: Language-model unlearning updates a trained model to behave as if it had not seen selected training examples, while preserving utility and avoiding costly retraining. Existing approaches typically fine-tune the pretrained model with a fixed training budget and select the final model afterwards by evaluating several saved checkpoints on downstream validation data. Two sources of unnecessary computation limit scalability: training beyond the desired forget-retain trade-off, and checkpoint selection that requires extra storage and repeated evaluations. To address these limitations, we introduce MArgin Self-Correction (MASC), an efficient unlearning method with an online stopping rule that does not require downstream evaluation. Given a text sequence to be forgotten, MASC actively reduces the logit gap between the original next token and the most likely alternatives. It outputs a final model once this gap is small on average over a sufficiently large proportion of token positions across all forget sequences. On TOFU, MUSE News, and MUSE Books, MASC achieves a competitive forget-retain trade-off at a fraction of the computational cost of existing baselines. We further observe that as we increase model size (a.k.a. number of parameters), the trade-offs improve for both MASC and SimNPO -- the forget metrics remain comparable while retain utility increases.

### [188] [Hierarchical RBF-KAN and RBF-SKAN Architectures for Multidimensional Function Approximation and Random Field Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02936)

Method: 采用径向基函数作为激活函数，构建分层Kolmogorov-Arnold网络结构（hierarchical RBF-KAN 和 hierarchical RBF-SKAN），结合函数分解思想降低有效维度，利用泛函分析工具进行逼近误差分析，并在理论与实验层面验证其性能。

Result: 理论证明了两种网络的通用逼近能力，分层RBF-KAN可实现对高维函数的高效逼近并缓解维数灾难；分层RBF-SKAN在Wasserstein-2度量下可有效逼近随机场模型；实验结果显示该方法在多变量函数和随机场学习任务中表现优异。

Conclusion: 所提出的分层RBF-KAN与RBF-SKAN架构在理论上具备良好的逼近性质，且在实践中展现出强大的函数与随机场建模能力，为高维数据学习提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: In this manuscript, we propose and analyze hierarchical Kolmogorov--Arnold neural network architectures employing radial basis functions as activation functions for approximating deterministic functions and random field models. Specifically, we develop a hierarchical radial-basis-function Kolmogorov--Arnold network (hierarchical RBF-KAN) for multidimensional deterministic function approximation and a hierarchical radial-basis-function stochastic Kolmogorov--Arnold network (hierarchical RBF-SKAN) for random field learning. From a theoretical perspective, we establish universal approximation results for both architectures. In particular, we derive quantitative approximation estimates for the hierarchical RBF-KAN, showing that the proposed framework has the potential to partially alleviate the curse of dimensionality in learning high-dimensional functions by reducing the effective dimensionality of the approximation problem. Furthermore, we show that the hierarchical RBF-SKAN can approximate random field models under the Wasserstein-2 metric. Empirically, we show that our proposed radial-basis-function-based neural network structure could effectively learn multivariate functions and random field models.

### [189] [ERP-XTTN: Interpretable Prototype-Guided Cross-Attention for Cross-Subject ERP Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02939)
*Charlotte Genevier Wyman,Leanne Hirshfield*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出ERP-XTTN，一种基于原型的跨注意力架构，用于在无需校准的情况下实现可解释的事件相关电位（ERP）分类。该方法通过查询-键仅有的交叉注意力机制将脑电信号片段路由至固定的差异波原型，使分类完全依赖于注意力路由，从而保证结构上的可解释性。原型由训练集差异波极值自动生成。在三个公开数据集（BNCI Horizon 2020、HRI Cursor、ERP CORE）上进行留一被试外评估，涵盖八种ERP成分，并在3通道与全导联条件下使用因果滤波器测试。结果表明，与EEGNet和xDAWN+RG等基线相比，ERP-XTTN在3通道下平均AUC差距为0.018，在全导联下为0.034，主要源于时间灵活性损失和空间利用不足。尽管精度略有下降，但其透明的注意力路由揭示了跨被试的神经信号结构，错误分类更接近真实阳性而非阴性，说明错误具有神经生理可解释性。该模型在最小导联数下实现了跨多种ERP的泛化能力，且具备良好可解释性。这是首次在ERP CORE上完成的分段级留一被试外基准测试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发一种无需校准、可解释且能在不同被试间有效泛化的脑机接口分类器，以解决当前在实际部署中面临的跨被试适应性和模型透明度问题。特别是针对事件相关电位（ERP）分类任务，现有黑箱模型难以提供神经生理层面的解释，而传统方法往往依赖个体校准，限制了实用性。因此，需要一种既能保持高性能又具备内在可解释性的新方法。

Method: 提出ERP-XTTN模型，采用仅查询-键的交叉注意力机制，将输入的脑电片段（EEG patches）映射到预先定义的差异波原型上，无值投影，确保分类过程仅由注意力路由决定。原型从训练数据中的差异波极值自动提取。在多数据集、多ERP成分、多通道配置下进行留一被试外评估，结合因果滤波处理，对比EEGNet和xDAWN+RG等基线模型。

Result: 在3通道条件下，ERP-XTTN相较于最佳基线平均提升0.018 AUROC；在全导联条件下提升0.034。性能差距主要来自两方面：与EEGNet相比存在时间灵活性损失，与xDAWN+RG相比存在空间利用不足，后者受信噪比影响显著。尽管精度略低，但模型展现出高度可解释性，其注意力路由能揭示跨被试的神经信号模式，错误分类更接近真实阳性，说明错误具有神经生理基础。该模型在无需校准、小导联配置下实现了对多种ERP成分的良好泛化能力。

Conclusion: ERP-XTTN是一种在无需校准、小导联条件下具有良好泛化能力的可解释型脑机接口分类器。它通过结构化的注意力路由机制实现了对跨被试ERP信号的透明建模，虽在某些场景下精度略逊于最优基线，但其可解释性显著优于现有黑箱方法。本研究首次建立了分段级的留一被试外基准测试，为未来可解释脑机接口的发展提供了重要参考。

Abstract: Interpretable brain-computer interface classifiers that generalize across subjects without calibration remain an open challenge. We test whether prototype-based cross-attention can provide competitive, interpretable event-related potential (ERP) classification under deployment-compatible conditions. We propose ERP-XTTN, a cross-attention architecture that routes input EEG patches to fixed difference-wave prototypes via query-key-only cross-attention with no value projection, so classification depends entirely on attention routing and attention faithfulness is structural rather than post-hoc. Prototypes are derived automatically from extrema in the training-fold difference wave. We evaluate across three public sources (BNCI Horizon 2020, HRI Cursor, and ERP CORE) spanning eight ERP components (ERN, LRP, ErrP, N170, P300, N2pc, MMN, N400), using leave-one-subject-out (LOSO) evaluation with causal filtering at two channel counts (3-channel and full montage), against EEGNet and xDAWN with Riemannian geometry (xDAWN+RG). The mean gap between the best baseline and ERP-XTTN was .018 AUROC at 3 channels and .034 at full montage, arising from two largely distinct sources: a temporal-flexibility cost relative to EEGNet and a spatial-exploitation cost relative to xDAWN+RG, the latter driven by signal-to-noise ratio at full montage. Beyond accuracy, the transparent routing reveals cross-subject signal structure that black-box models cannot: false positives resembled true positives more than true negatives did, indicating that classification errors are neurophysiologically explicable. ERP-XTTN generalizes across diverse ERPs under causal, calibration-free conditions with a small interpretability cost at minimal montages. To our knowledge, this is the first epoch-level LOSO benchmark on ERP CORE.

### [190] [Outsmarting the Chameleon: Counterfactual Decoupling for Tactical OOD Shifts in Live Streaming Risk Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02946)
*Yiran Qiao,Jing Chen,Jiaqi Xu,Yang Liu,Qiwei Zhong,Xiang Ao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Latent-Predictive Counterfactual Decoupling (LPCD) 框架，通过在潜在空间中分离恶意意图与叙事表现，建立反事实一致性约束，并在推理阶段采用轻量级、无参数校准机制进一步缓解因战术变化引起的分布偏移。

Result: 在大规模工业数据集和真实线上流量上的实验表明，LPCD显著优于当前最先进的基线方法，在持续演化的对抗风险下展现出更强的鲁棒性和实用性。

Conclusion: LPCD为直播风险评估提供了一个高效且可扩展的解决方案，其核心在于将因果稳定性引入反事实推理，有效应对战术性对抗性包装，适用于复杂动态的真实世界场景。

Abstract: Live streaming has emerged as a primary medium for social interaction and digital commerce, yet it is increasingly plagued by sophisticated risks. A fundamental challenge in this domain is \emph{tactical out-of-distribution (OOD) shift}: while malicious actors maintain stable underlying objectives, they continuously redesign narrative packaging to evade detection. Such adversarial shifts expose critical limitations of existing OOD generalization paradigms, whose assumptions are difficult to satisfy in the presence of tightly coupled intent-tactic evolution and ill-defined raw-level counterfactuals.
  In this paper, we tackle this issue from a \emph{latent causal} perspective and propose \underline{L}atent-\underline{P}redictive \underline{C}ounterfactual \underline{D}ecoupling~(LPCD), a plug-in framework for robust live streaming risk assessment. LPCD enables counterfactual reasoning under adversarial tactical re-packaging by modeling intent and narrative variation at the latent level, and enforces \emph{latent counterfactual consistency} to anchor risk prediction on causally stable malicious intent. At inference time, LPCD applies a lightweight, parameter-free calibration to further mitigate tactic-induced distribution shifts. Extensive experiments on large-scale industrial datasets and online production traffic demonstrate that LPCD consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, validating its effectiveness in moderating evolving adversarial risks in real-world live streaming. The project page is available at https://qiaoyran.github.io/LiveStreamingRiskAssessment/.

### [191] [BYORn: Bootstrap Your Own Responses to Defend Large Vision-Language Models Against Backdoor Attacks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02947)
*Ivan Sabolić,Marin Oršić,Josip Šarić,Sven Lončarić*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: BYORn 是一种针对自回归视觉-语言模型后门攻击的鲁棒微调框架，通过识别语义不一致的目标响应并动态替换为模型生成的替代响应，打破触发器与目标输出之间的关联，从而提升对后门攻击的防御能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有监督微调方法在下游任务中极易受到后门攻击，且现有防御手段在开放式生成场景下无效，因此需要一种更鲁棒的微调策略。

Method: BYORn 通过检测输入图像-文本与目标响应之间的语义不一致性，动态替换不合理的响应，利用模型自身生成替代输出，使梯度反映干净数据分布上的经验风险上界。

Result: 实验表明，BYORn 在保持良好清洁任务性能的同时，显著提升了对后门攻击的鲁棒性，并在面对自适应攻击时仍具有效性，建立了新的泛化与攻击成功率之间的权衡前沿。

Conclusion: BYORn 提供了一种有效且稳健的微调框架，能够抵御多种后门攻击，尤其适用于开放生成场景下的视觉-语言模型安全应用。

Abstract: Supervised fine-tuning is the predominant approach for adapting autoregressive vision-language models to downstream tasks. Recent work has shown that this paradigm is highly vulnerable to backdoor attacks, and that existing defenses are ineffective in open-ended generation settings. In response, we propose BYORn, a backdoor-robust fine-tuning framework motivated by the observation that poisoned target responses are often semantically implausible given the corresponding image-text inputs and a pretrained model. BYORn identifies such misaligned responses and dynamically replaces them with alternative responses generated by the model, thereby breaking the correlation between triggers and target outputs. The resulting objective gradient corresponds to the gradient of the empirical estimate of the population risk upper bound over the clean data distribution. Empirically, BYORn consistently improves robustness to backdoor attacks while preserving clean-task performance, establishing a new trade-off frontier between generalization and attack success rate. Finally, we demonstrate that BYORn remains effective against adaptive attacks specifically designed to circumvent the proposed defense.

</details>


### [192] [From Non-Convex to Strongly Convex: Curvature-Adaptive FTPL for Online Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02948)
*Moses Charikar,Chirag Pabbaraju,Ambuj Tewari*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了在线优化中的曲率自适应问题，提出了一种改进的跟随扰动领导者（FTPL）算法，在非凸利普希茨损失下实现曲率自适应，无需预先知道曲率累积情况。通过引入基于历史信息的时间可变扰动尺度，新算法在任意非凸情况下达到 $O(\sqrt{T})$ 的后悔界，并在累积曲率增大时表现更优；当累积曲率线性增长时（如强凸情形），可达到 $O(\log T)$ 的快速收敛率。作者还给出了匹配的下界，证明这种在最坏情况与曲率驱动快率之间的权衡是内在的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统自适应方法在非凸设置中无法利用曲率信息，尽管已有工作表明标准FTPL在非凸情况下能实现最优 $O(\sqrt{T})$ 的后悔界，但未考虑曲率的影响。因此，迫切需要一种能够在不事先知晓曲率演化的情况下，自动利用曲率信息以获得更快收敛速度的方法。

Method: 提出一种改进的FTPL算法，用时间可变的扰动尺度替代原有的固定尺度，该尺度由过去的信息决定，并采用简单的跟随领导者规则进行调节。这种方法使得算法能够动态响应累积曲率的变化，从而在不同曲率条件下自适应地调整性能。

Result: 所提算法在任意非凸利普希茨损失下保证 $O(\sqrt{T})$ 后悔界，且随着累积曲率的增长而改善；当累积曲率线性增长时，若近似离线优化器足够精确，则可实现 $O(\log T)$ 的后悔界。同时，对指定累积曲率序列，建立了匹配的下界，验证了该性能权衡的固有性。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了在非凸设置下，通过设计合适的时间可变扰动策略，可以在不依赖先验曲率信息的前提下实现曲率自适应，显著提升了算法的实用性与理论性能边界。

Abstract: Curvature adaptivity is a classical theme in online optimization: for convex Lipschitz losses, adaptive methods interpolate between the optimal $O(\sqrt{T})$ regret for general convex losses and $O(\log T)$ regret under strong convexity. Recent work has shown that Follow-the-Perturbed-Leader (FTPL) achieves optimal $O(\sqrt{T})$ regret even for online non-convex Lipschitz losses, assuming access to an approximate offline-optimization oracle, but these guarantees do not exploit curvature. We show that FTPL can be made curvature-adaptive in the non-convex setting, without knowing in advance how curvature will accumulate over time. Our algorithm replaces the fixed perturbation scale of standard FTPL with a time-varying scale chosen using only past information. We give a simple follow-the-leader tuning rule for this scale and show that it competes, up to constants, with the best choice in hindsight. The resulting method achieves $O(\sqrt{T})$ regret for arbitrary non-convex Lipschitz losses and improves as cumulative curvature grows; with sufficiently accurate oracle calls, it achieves $O(\log T)$ regret when cumulative curvature grows linearly, which includes the classical strongly convex regime. We complement these upper bounds with matching lower bounds for prescribed cumulative-curvature sequences, already for one-dimensional convex losses, showing that the tradeoff between worst-case non-convex regret and curvature-driven fast rates is intrinsic.

</details>


### [193] [Gate AI: LLM Security Benchmark Evaluation Methodology and Results](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02959)
*Ryle Goehausen,Marcus Sousa*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种评估大语言模型提示注入和越狱检测器的改进框架，通过统一全局操作点、跨数据集交叉验证和多种诊断方法，解决了传统评估中阈值调优和操作点不透明的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法存在每数据集独立调优阈值和操作点不透明的问题，影响结果可比性和泛化能力评估。

Method: 采用5折交叉验证，在16个公开基准上评估检测器；使用StratifiedKFold和StratifiedGroupKFold（基于父提示ID与MinHash+LSH近似重复聚类）并行运行，以防止数据泄露；选择单一全局操作点（最大化F1且假阳性率≤1%），并在所有数据集上统一应用；通过多种诊断手段检验泛化性。

Result: 该评估框架能更公平、一致地比较不同检测器性能，有效揭示模型在不同场景下的鲁棒性和泛化能力，并支持在相同操作点下进行横向对比。

Conclusion: 该评估框架显著提升了提示注入和越狱检测器评估的严谨性与可比性，为未来研究提供了可靠基准。

Abstract: Published evaluations of prompt-injection and jailbreak detectors for Large Language Models often suffer from two systematic weaknesses: per-dataset threshold tuning and undisclosed operating points. We describe an evaluation harness that addresses both. The detector under evaluation is scored across 16 public benchmarks (12,111 samples) using 5-fold cross-validation. StratifiedKFold (by row) is the headline pass; a parallel StratifiedGroupKFold pass over a composite key (parent-prompt id plus MinHash + LSH near-duplicate clusters at Jaccard $\gtrsim 0.8$) runs alongside it as a leakage-premium diagnostic. A single global operating point is selected on the held-out folds (max F1 subject to FPR $\leq 1\%$) and applied uniformly to every dataset, so per-dataset results reflect one threshold rather than per-benchmark optimisation. Generalisation is examined through a battery of diagnostics (leave-one-dataset-out cross-validation, a random-label control, adversarial validation, permutation feature importance, length-bias correlation, classifier-head agreement, cross-source near-duplicate detection, threshold transferability, train-vs-OOF agreement, and a paraphrase-invariance probe), most with a quantitative pass threshold and the remainder with a stated failure mode. For every external comparison, the detector's threshold is re-tuned to the competitor's published false-positive rate so head-to-head values are evaluated at matched operating points.

### [194] [KForge: LLM-Driven Cross-Platform Kernel Generation for AI Accelerators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02963)
*Taras Sereda,Burak Bartan,Ankita Nayak,Tom St. John,Natalie Serrino,Zain Asgar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: KForge是一个跨平台框架，通过两个协作的LLM代理驱动的迭代优化循环，实现自动生成高效、正确的硬件特定内核。该框架在NVIDIA B200和Intel Arc B580上分别实现了2.12%的吞吐量提升和5.13倍的几何平均加速，主要得益于算子融合和混合精度执行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生产环境中的推理任务日益依赖异构加速器，且智能体流水线涉及推理、工具调用和多智能体协同，各阶段对计算和内存需求不同。为实现最佳效率，每个阶段需部署在最合适的硬件上，但手动编写适配多种后端的高性能内核耗时且难以扩展。现有基于LLM的自动内核生成方法仍面临底层代码生成和跨平台泛化能力不足的问题。

Method: KForge采用双代理机制：生成代理负责根据编译和正确性反馈逐步优化内核；性能分析代理则解析性能剖析数据（包括程序接口与图形化工具），提出优化建议以指导下一阶段合成。系统在功能验证与性能优化之间交替迭代，实现从功能性到高性能的渐进式改进。

Result: 在NVIDIA B200上，KForge相比TensorRT-LLM在gpt-oss-20b基准测试中提升了2.12%的端到端吞吐量；在Intel Arc B580上，其生成的Triton内核在37个GEMM+尾操作工作负载上相较PyTorch eager和torch.compile最快版本平均提速5.13倍，主要归因于算子融合和混合精度执行。

Conclusion: KForge通过智能的迭代优化机制，有效解决了跨平台内核生成中功能正确性与性能优化的双重挑战，显著降低开发成本并提升异构推理系统的整体效率。

Abstract: Production inference increasingly targets a heterogeneous mix of accelerators. Agentic pipelines interleave reasoning, tool calls, and multi-agent coordination, each with distinct compute and memory profiles. For optimal efficiency, each stage should run on the accelerator best suited to it. This creates a systems challenge: each pipeline now requires high-performance kernels across a growing set of hardware backends and programming models. Writing these kernels by hand is time-consuming, demands deep low-level expertise, and does not scale as kernel complexity grows. Recently, Large Language Models (LLMs) have been leveraged for automatic kernel generation, but challenges in low-level code generation and cross-backend generalization persist. We present KForge, a cross-platform framework built around an iterative refinement loop driven by two collaborating LLM-based agents: a generation agent that produces and progressively refines kernels using compilation and correctness feedback, and a performance-analysis agent that interprets profiling data, from programmatic APIs to GUI-based tools, and emits recommendations that steer the next round of synthesis. The loop alternates between functional passes, which drive a candidate to correctness, and optimization passes, which close the performance gap to hand-tuned baselines. We evaluate KForge on two backends with very different baseline reference availability. On NVIDIA B200, KForge achieves a 2.12$\%$ improvement in end-to-end throughput compared to TensorRT-LLM on the gpt-oss-20b inference speed benchmark. On Intel Arc B580, KForge generates Triton kernels achieving a 5.13$\times$ geometric mean speedup over the faster of PyTorch eager and torch.compile on 37 GEMM + tail-ops workloads from KernelBench Level 2, primarily via operator fusion and mixed-precision execution.

### [195] [Neural Networks Provably Learn Spectral Representations for Group Composition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02993)
*Jianliang He,Leda Wang,Fengzhuo Zhang,Siyu Chen,Zhuoran Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了神经网络训练中结构化内部结构的涌现机制，通过群组合任务（预测有限群G中元素的运算结果）分析两层神经网络的训练动态。通过将投影梯度流提升到傅里叶域，发现训练过程遵循表示论能量泛函上的黎曼梯度上升。在随机初始化下，几乎必然地，每个神经元收敛至单一不可约表示，跨层傅里叶系数实现旋转秩一对齐。该框架提供了特征学习的表示论解释，并揭示了一种矩阵值群表示的新低秩压缩现象。对于阿贝尔群，给出了完整的群体层面描述：随机初始化促进非平凡表示的均匀分散和哈尔均匀相位，通过多数投票机制近似指示函数。同时证明相位对齐与表示竞争以指数速率出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将投影梯度流提升至傅里叶域，分析其在表示论能量泛函上的黎曼梯度上升行为；利用随机初始化下的概率分析，研究神经元收敛与跨层系数对齐的性质。

Result: 在随机初始化下，神经元几乎必然收敛至单一不可约表示，跨层傅里叶系数实现旋转秩一对齐；对于阿贝尔群，呈现均匀表示分布与哈尔均匀相位，通过多数投票近似指示函数；相位对齐与表示竞争均以指数速率发生。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一个基于表示论的神经网络特征学习理论框架，揭示了训练过程中的低秩压缩机制，并阐明了群结构如何影响表示学习的演化路径。

Abstract: Understanding how structured internal structure emerges during neural network training is central to the study of deep learning. We investigate this phenomenon through the group composition task, where a two-layer neural network is trained to predict $g_1 \star g_2$ for elements of a finite group $G$. By lifting the projected gradient flow to the Fourier domain, we demonstrate that the training dynamics are governed by a Riemannian gradient ascent on a representation-theoretic energy functional. We prove that, under random initialization, this flow drives each neuron to converge almost surely toward a single irreducible representation, while the cross-layer Fourier coefficients achieve a rotational rank-one alignment. This framework provides a representation-theoretic account of feature learning and characterizes a novel low-rank compression phenomenon for matrix-valued group representations. Moreover, for Abelian groups, we provide a complete population-level description: random initialization promotes uniform diversification across nontrivial representations and induces Haar-uniform phases, jointly approximating the indicator via a majority-vote mechanism. We further prove that both phase alignment and representation competition emerge with exponential convergence rates.

### [196] [CoughSense: Five-Class Respiratory Disease Classification via Whisper Encoder Fine-Tuning and Dual-Encoder Cross-Attention Fusion with Balanced Contrastive Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02998)
*Nikhil Vincent*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CoughSense 是一个基于 Whisper 编码器的咳嗽分析系统，可将咳嗽录音分类为健康、新冠、哮喘/呼吸系统疾病、支气管炎和肺炎五类。通过主动帧 QKV 注意力池化解决短音频在长输入窗口中的静音稀释问题，并结合多种技术应对类别不平衡与跨数据集域偏移问题。该系统在五折交叉验证中达到 82.3% 的平衡准确率，显著优于其他模型，且主动帧池化是性能提升的关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有咳嗽分析多仅限于二分类（如是否感染新冠），缺乏对多种呼吸疾病的综合识别能力。为实现低成本、高精度的智能手机端呼吸疾病筛查，需构建能区分多种呼吸病症的实用系统。

Method: 采用 OpenAI Whisper-tiny 作为预训练主干网络，引入主动帧 QKV 注意力池化，仅关注前 200 个编码器标记以避免静音稀释；结合 WeightedRandomSampler、SpecAugment、Balanced Mixup、监督对比辅助损失、FiLM 症状条件化及梯度反转域适应处理数据不平衡与域偏移；设计双编码器结构融合 Whisper 与 OPERA-CT 基础模型，通过交叉注意力融合特征。

Result: CoughSense 在五类分类任务中达到 82.3% 平衡准确率（宏 F1 0.817，AUC 0.941），优于 ImageNet 预训练 EfficientNet-B2（+11.1%）和从零训练的 ViT（+29.6%）。所有类别召回率均超过 74%，四类超过 80%。双编码器版本进一步提升至 85.4% 平衡准确率。主动帧池化贡献最大，提升 5.1 个百分点。

Conclusion: CoughSense 成功实现了多类呼吸疾病从单次咳嗽录音中的精准分类，尤其在短音频任务中利用 Whisper 主干具有显著优势。主动帧注意力建议可推广至其他类似任务，具备实际部署潜力。

Abstract: Automated cough analysis offers a path to low-cost respiratory screening, but most existing work stops at binary COVID-19 detection. A practical tool needs to tell apart several respiratory conditions from one cough recording on a consumer smartphone. We present CoughSense, a system that sorts cough recordings into five classes. These are healthy, COVID-19, asthma or respiratory condition, bronchitis, and pneumonia. We aggregated 18,301 recordings from four public datasets (Coswara, CoughVID, Virufy, and the West China Hospital Pediatric Cough Dataset) and used the OpenAI Whisper encoder as a pretrained backbone for cough disease classification. The main contribution is active-frame QKV attention pooling, which restricts attention to the first 200 of 1500 encoder tokens. This avoids the silence-dilution problem that arises because a 3-second cough fills only 150 tokens of Whisper's 30-second input window. Other training parts handle the 19 to 1 class imbalance and the four-dataset domain shift. These include WeightedRandomSampler, SpecAugment, Balanced Mixup with forced minority pairing, a supervised contrastive auxiliary loss, FiLM symptom conditioning, and gradient-reversal domain adaptation. A dual-encoder model fuses Whisper with the OPERA-CT respiratory foundation model through cross-attention. CoughSense (Whisper-tiny, 8.6M parameters) reached 82.3 percent balanced accuracy on five-fold cross-validation (macro-F1 of 0.817, AUC of 0.941). It beat an ImageNet-pretrained EfficientNet-B2 by 11.1 points and a ViT trained from scratch by 29.6 points. All five classes passed 74 percent recall and four of five passed 80 percent. The dual-encoder model reached 85.4 percent balanced accuracy. Active-frame pooling is the largest single contributor across all ablation components at 5.1 points, which should help any short-audio task using Whisper as a backbone.

### [197] [How Quantization Changes Interpretable Features: A Sparse Autoencoder Analysis of Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03002)
*Evan Duan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了量化对大语言模型中稀疏自编码器（SAE）特征保留的影响，发现特征衰减是渐进的而非突然崩溃，且可通过全精度统计预测。尽管任务指标（如困惑度）未显示异常，但部分特征已受损，表明行为一致性不足以保证可解释性成果在量化部署中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量化评估主要依赖于困惑度或下游任务准确率，但忽略了模型内部可解释特征是否在量化后依然保持一致。随着安全审计和控制干预越来越依赖这些特征，确保其在量化后的存活至关重要。

Method: 使用冻结的SAE作为固定测量基准，对Pythia-70M和Gemma-2-2B模型在不同位宽（从INT8到INT4）下的全精度与四舍五入量化（RTN）激活进行编码，并通过皮尔逊相关系数衡量每项特征的生存率。同时分析了跨模型的特征损伤重叠及预测能力。

Result: 特征生存呈渐进式下降，在INT6下，Pythia-70M有62.4%的活跃特征存活，Gemma-2-2B为51.3%；多数非存活特征表现为模糊而非彻底消失。特征生存可由全精度统计预测，交叉验证AUC达0.92–0.97，峰值激活是最强预测因子。值得注意的是，即使在任务性能提升（如INT7提升困惑度）的情况下，仍有18.7%特征受损。量化与匹配困惑度的幅度剪枝在特征损伤上高度重叠（Jaccard重合度0.79–0.86），且损伤评分高度相关（Spearman相关系数0.98）。

Conclusion: 仅依靠行为一致性（如任务性能）无法保证可解释性特征在量化模型中的转移。必须引入特征层面的审计机制，以确保模型压缩过程不会破坏关键解释结构。

Abstract: Quantization is a standard path to deploying large language models, and a quantized model is typically judged acceptable when its perplexity or downstream accuracy stays close to the full-precision original. Whether the model still computes in the same way, or whether the interpretable features identified in the full-precision model survive weight rounding, is rarely tested, even as safety audits and steering interventions increasingly rely on those features. We ask whether sparse autoencoder (SAE) features extracted from a dense full-precision model remain faithful once that model is quantized. Using a frozen SAE as a fixed measurement basis, we encode full-precision and round-to-nearest (RTN) quantized activations on identical tokens and quantify per-feature survival by Pearson correlation, sweeping bit-widths from INT8 to INT4 on Pythia-70M and Gemma-2-2B. We find that feature survival is graded: features degrade systematically rather than failing all at once, with 62.4 percent of active features surviving at INT6 on Pythia-70M and 51.3 percent surviving at INT6 on Gemma-2-2B, and with most non-survivors blurred rather than destroyed. Survival is predictable from full-precision statistics alone, with cross-validated AUCs of 0.92 to 0.97 and peak activation as the strongest marginal predictor. Critically, task metrics can miss this damage: on Gemma-2-2B, INT7 improves perplexity while degrading 18.7 percent of features. Finally, quantization and matched-perplexity magnitude pruning damage strongly overlapping feature sets, with Jaccard overlap of 0.79 to 0.86 and damage-score Spearman correlation of 0.98, suggesting a shared mode of compression-induced vulnerability. These results show that behavioral parity is insufficient evidence that interpretability findings transfer to quantized deployments, motivating feature-level audits of compression.

</details>


### [198] [Exact equivariance, kept through training, buys zero-shot generalisation across the symmetry group](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03003)
*Hongbo Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出一种基于等变编码器 $E$ 和等变预测器 $f$ 构建的潜在世界模型，其训练损失具有可证明的对称性：当世界动力学真实携带群 $G$ 作用于潜变量并由正交表示 $ρ(g)$ 描述时，单步预测相对均方误差（relMSE）在整个群上精确不变，这意味着在受限方向片上拟合动力学即可数学上确定整个轨道上的动力学行为。实验验证了这一性质在笔记本规模（CPU/MPS，完全可复现）下的有效性，并展示了等变模型在多个维度下显著优于非等变基线（2D: VN×1.00 vs baseline×13.8；3D: ×17.2；SE(3)全阶梯: ×157），且等变模型误差小4.5–7.4倍。进一步地，等变性在闭环控制中保持：匹配的等变规划器使得在不同方向上的控制轨迹恰好是已见轨迹的 $ρ(g)$ 变换，因此闭环误差在群上保持不变，在2D/ SO(2) 上达到浮点精度精确，3D/ SE(3) 上统计平坦。该方法经受住Sutton“苦涩教训”的考验——数据增强、暴力扩展和软等变性均无法达到这种浮点级精确性。由于等变性在复合下封闭，$H$-步滚动预测误差始终保持平坦（×1.00，≤2×10⁻⁷），而基线误差随 $H$ 增长。研究未涵盖任务成功率分析、无规划器的不变性以及扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界模型在处理具有对称性的物理系统时，往往因缺乏显式等变性而导致泛化能力受限，尤其在跨方向或姿态的外推性能差。本文旨在通过引入严格等变结构，实现从有限观测到完整对称轨道的精确外推，从而突破传统方法在对称性建模上的瓶颈。

Method: 设计一个由等变编码器 $E$ 和等变预测器 $f$ 组成的潜在世界模型，利用群 $G$ 的正交表示 $ρ(g)$ 对潜空间进行变换，确保模型预测在群作用下保持不变。通过构建等变损失函数与等变规划器，实现从单步预测到多步闭环控制的全程对称性保障。采用真实优化器（MuOne/AdamW + EMA + VICReg）进行训练，并在 PushT 任务上进行端到端验证。

Result: 在2D和3D环境中，等变模型的单步预测误差在群内保持平坦（五位有效数字），远优于非等变基线（误差高出10倍以上）；闭环控制误差在2D/ SO(2) 上为浮点精度精确，在3D/ SE(3) 上统计平坦；$H$-步滚动预测误差始终稳定（≤2×10⁻⁷），而基线误差随 $H$ 指数增长。

Conclusion: 等变世界模型通过显式建模对称性，实现了从局部观测到全局对称轨道的精确外推，其预测与控制误差在群作用下保持精确不变。该方法不仅超越了当前主流的增强与缩放策略，还具备理论保证与实证支持，为高对称性系统的建模提供了新范式。

Abstract: A latent world model built from an equivariant encoder $E$ and an equivariant predictor $f$ inherits a provable symmetry of its training loss: when the world's dynamics genuinely carries a group $G$ acting on latents by an orthogonal representation $ρ(g)$, the one-step prediction relMSE is exactly invariant across the whole group, so fitting the dynamics on a restricted slice of orientations mathematically determines it on the entire orbit (jǔ yī fǎn sān). We verify this end-to-end at laptop scale (CPU/MPS, fully seeded). [A] The symmetry survives a real Muon/AdamW + EMA + VICReg run -- composed encode-then-predict residual $\sim 10^{-6}$ after optimisation, not just at initialisation, and under any optimiser. [B] One-step error is flat to five digits across the group, while a same-hypothesis-class non-equivariant baseline fits the slice but breaks out-of-distribution (VN $\times 1.00$ vs baseline $\times 13.8$ in 2D, $\times 17.2$ in 3D, $\times 157$ over the full $\mathrm{SE}(3)$ ladder), with the equivariant model $4.5$-$7.4\times$ smaller. [C] The same isometry argument lifts to closed loop: under a matching equivariant planner the control trajectory at orientation $g$ is exactly $ρ(g)$ applied to the seen one, so closed-loop error is invariant across the group -- float-floor-exact in 2D/$\mathrm{SO}(2)$ on real PushT and statistically flat in 3D/$\mathrm{SE}(3)$ (disjoint 95% CIs). We stress-test the prior against Sutton's Bitter Lesson: augmentation, brute-force scale, and soft-equivariance each close at most the across-group task metric, never the float-floor exactness. Because equivariance is closed under composition, the $H$-fold rollout stays flat ($\times 1.00$, $\le 2\times 10^{-7}$) at every horizon, while the baseline's residual compounds with $H$. Out of scope: task-success sweeps, planner-free invariance, and scaling.

</details>


### [199] [MOSAIC: Efficient Mixture-of-Agent Scheduling via Adaptive Aggregation and Inference Concurrency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03014)
*Saptarshi Mitra,Yifan Zhang,Rachid Karami,Phyo Pyae Moe Aung,Nazmul Takbir,Sreetama Sarkar,Souvik Kundu,Sitao Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MOSAIC 是一种用于加速混合专家（MoA）工作负载的调度框架，通过联合优化专家部署和提示分配，并采用基于置信度的自适应聚合策略，有效缓解了资源瓶颈与负载不均问题。在4-GPU系统中，相比基线调度器，实现了最高2.5倍的专家阶段、4.23倍的聚合阶段以及1.7~2.3倍的端到端速度提升，同时保持精度损失小于0.1个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统调度策略在处理MoA系统时面临专家需求偏斜和生成长度波动大导致的GPU空闲与吞吐量下降问题，亟需高效调度机制以提升资源利用率和推理效率。

Method: 提出基于整数线性规划（ILP）的调度器，结合离线性能分析结果，实现专家跨工作节点复制与轻量级专家固定部署；引入置信度感知的自适应聚合机制，利用专家间一致性判断是否跳过重型聚合模型。

Conclusion: MOSAIC通过智能调度与动态聚合策略，显著提升了MoA系统的执行效率，在保证高准确率的前提下大幅改善了GPU资源利用率与系统吞吐能力。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Agents (MoA) systems improve reasoning accuracy by routing each query to multiple expert LLMs and aggregating their outputs. Efficiently executing this workload on limited GPU resources has bottlenecks. Skill-based routing creates skewed expert demand, and combining instruction-tuned LLMs with long-reasoning models results in extreme variability in generation lengths. Consequently, traditional scheduling strategies suffer from significant GPU idling and throughput collapse due to load imbalances. We present MOSAIC, a scheduling framework to accelerate MoA workloads. First, we formulate an Integer Linear Program (ILP) based scheduler that jointly optimizes expert placement and per-worker prompt assignment from offline-profiled costs, replicating reasoning experts across workers while pinning lightweight ones. Second, MOSAIC uses confidence-aware adaptive aggregation, leveraging inter-expert agreement to bypass the heavy final aggregator LLM for consensus queries. In our 4-GPU system, MOSAIC achieves up to 2.5x expert-stage, 4.23x aggregator-stage and 1.7~2.3x end-to-end speedups over the baseline scheduler, while matching accuracy within 0.1pp.

### [200] [ConTraIRL: Factorized Contrastive Abstractions for Transferable IRL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03017)
*Yikang Gui,Bikramjit Banerjee,Prashant Doshi*

TL;DR: ConTraIRL 提出一种新的逆强化学习框架，通过解耦环境动态和任务目标的潜在表示，实现可迁移的奖励转移。其双编码器架构结合对比学习，分别学习与目标无关的动态结构和与动态无关的目标特征，支持在未见的动态-目标组合上进行有效奖励推断。实验表明，在连续控制任务中，该方法在少样本迁移场景下显著提升样本效率和奖励恢复性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在逆强化学习中，当策略需要泛化到未见过的环境动态和任务目标组合时，传统的奖励转移方法不可靠。因此，亟需一种能够解耦动态和目标因素并支持组合泛化的奖励迁移机制。

Method: 提出基于双编码器的对比学习框架 ConTraIRL，分别将观测映射至动态和目标的潜在空间；通过时间对齐和双重对比损失，强制动态编码器学习目标无关结构，目标编码器捕捉动态无关特征，从而实现因子解耦。

Result: 在多个连续控制基准测试中，ConTraIRL 在未见的动态-目标组合上实现了有效的少样本迁移，相比现有转移 IRL 方法，显著提升了样本效率和奖励恢复准确率。

Conclusion: ConTraIRL 通过学习解耦的动态与目标潜在表示，有效解决了逆强化学习中的跨组合迁移问题，为复杂任务下的奖励泛化提供了新范式。

Abstract: Reward transfer in Inverse Reinforcement Learning (IRL) is unreliable when policies must generalize to unseen combinations of environment dynamics and task goals. We propose Factorized Contrastive Abstractions for Transferable IRL (ConTraIRL), a framework that enables compositional reward transfer by learning decoupled latent representations of these two factors. ConTraIRL uses a dual-encoder architecture that maps observations into separate dynamics and goal latent spaces, trained with a dual contrastive objective. Temporal alignment encourages the dynamics encoder to learn goal-invariant structure, while the goal encoder captures dynamics-invariant features. This factorization supports reward inference under recombined dynamics-goal settings. Experiments on continuous control benchmarks demonstrate effective few-shot transfer to unseen dynamics-goal pairings, improving sample efficiency and reward recovery over transfer IRL baselines.

### [201] [Will Accurate Fields Mislead Photonic Design? FromGlobal Accuracy to Port Readout](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03038)
*Yitian Zhang,Yonghong chen,Youming Chen,Yiyang Li,Xing Zhe,Renhe Lu,Shaolin Liao,Yuzhe Ma,Zhong Guan*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 全局场误差不足以保证设计相关读数的准确性；通过显式建模传播路径与输出窗口聚合过程，能够显著提升代理模型在实际设计任务中的可靠性与实用性。

Abstract: Neural field surrogates can accelerate photonic design loops, but a surrogate that looks accurate in global field error can still mis-rank candidate devices when the final decision depends on localized output-port readouts. This risk is acute in propagation-dominated MMI splitters and couplers, where port power, splitting, phase, and coupling are determined by accumulated modal interference and output-window aggregation rather than by average field similarity alone. We study this field-to-design mismatch through a Field/Mediator/Readout view that separates dense complex-field error from propagation-profile and output-window errors before port aggregation. To align the surrogate with this chain, we propose PaNO, a propagation-aligned neural operator that keeps the full-field prediction interface while organizing latent states around local boundary structure, transverse modal content, axial propagation, and cross-mode interaction. We also evaluate PaNO-R2, an output-aware feedback variant for residual field components near the port region. On a 15-wavelength tunable $3{\times}3$ MMI benchmark with 4608 held-out fields, PaNO lowers NeurOLight's port-power error from 0.2018 to 0.0739 despite slightly higher cMAE, showing that global field accuracy alone is not sufficient for design-relevant readout fidelity. PaNO-R2 attains the best cMAE, propagation-profile error, output-profile error, and port-power error, reducing NeurOLight's port-power and output-profile errors by 72.7\% and 72.5\%.

### [202] [What Do Students Learn? A Feature-Level Analysis of Dark Knowledge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03052)
*Seungu Kang,Songkuk Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过交互张量框架分析知识蒸馏中学生模型的特征学习机制，发现有效知识蒸馏可作为正则化手段，剔除低频、样本特异的特征，促使学生模型依赖一组高度可复用的紧凑特征。研究进一步发现数据集级别的混淆矩阵蕴含类似教师模型'暗知识'的结构信息，据此提出无需教师模型的自蒸馏方法Confusion Distillation（CD），利用模型自身演化的混淆模式作为动态软目标。CD在CIFAR-100上对ResNet-34和ResNet-50表现优异，性能优于CS-KD和PS-KD等现有自蒸馏方法1.2%，且计算效率高于标准知识蒸馏。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 知识蒸馏本质上是一种正则化机制，能引导学生模型聚焦于高可复用的特征；利用模型自身混淆模式作为软目标的自蒸馏方法（CD）不仅有效，而且高效，为无教师知识蒸馏提供了新思路。

Abstract: Knowledge Distillation (KD) is a powerful tool for model compression, yet the precise mechanisms by which student models acquire feature representations remain underexplored. In this work, we analyze student feature learning using the Interaction Tensor framework. Our analysis reveals that effective KD acts as a regularizer that prunes low-frequency, sample-specific features, encouraging the student to rely on a compact set of highly reusable features. Crucially, we observe that the dataset-level confusion matrix contains structural information analogous to the teacher's "Dark Knowledge." Leveraging this insight, we propose Confusion Distillation (CD), a teacher-free self-distillation method that utilizes the model's own evolving confusion patterns as dynamic soft targets. ### [203] [Rethinking Molecular Text Representations for LLMs: An Empirical Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03057)
*Arun Raja,Garrett M. Morris,Kian Ming A. Chai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究系统评估了九种分子表示法在八项化学任务中对大语言模型（LLMs）的性能影响，发现不同表示法在不同任务上表现差异显著，其中CML表现最佳，其次是MolJSON、InChI和标准SMILES。结构化文本表示（如CML和MolJSON）在结构类任务中占优，而IUPAC在语义任务中表现最佳，尤其在分子检索任务中对所有16个模型均胜出。尽管SMILES在预训练中广泛使用，但其并非最优选择。专业化学模型虽在SMILES上表现良好，但在结构化表示上性能大幅下降，表明仅用SMILES评估会奖励特定性而非泛化能力。通过LLM作为裁判的评估，IUPAC生成正确分子的比例最高。机制分析显示，不同表示法在模型内部编码方式不同，结构化表示需要更高的注意力跨度。研究主张避免表示无关的评估，提倡基于任务的表示路由策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 明确大语言模型在分子任务中的表现受分子表示方法影响，现有评估缺乏对表示法的系统比较，且多数研究依赖于普遍使用的SMILES表示，可能掩盖了其他表示的优势或局限，因此亟需全面评估不同表示法的适用性和性能差异。

Method: 系统性基准测试：在九种分子表示法（如SMILES、InChI、CML、MolJSON、IUPAC等）和八项化学任务（如分子生成、检索、属性预测等）上，对16个大语言模型（涵盖五类模型家族，包括推理与非推理变体、化学专用模型、闭源前沿模型）进行评估。采用人工评估与自动化指标结合的方式，并引入LLM-as-a-judge进行生成质量判断。进一步通过分词审计、线性探测和注意力分析等机制研究手段，揭示不同表示法在模型内部的编码特性差异。

Result: CML是综合表现最佳的表示法，其次为MolJSON、InChI和标准SMILES；结构化文本表示在结构任务中占优，IUPAC在语义任务（尤其是分子检索）中全面领先；SMILES虽常见于预训练数据，但并非最优，且化学专用模型在SMILES上表现好但对结构化表示适应差，表现出严重的泛化缺陷；使用LLM作为裁判时，IUPAC生成的分子正确率最高；机制分析显示不同表示法在模型中被以不同方式编码，结构化表示需要更长的注意力跨度。

Conclusion: 应摒弃对分子表示法的表示无关评估，倡导根据具体任务选择最优表示法，提出任务感知的表示路由策略，以提升大语言模型在化学领域的应用效能。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used for molecular tasks, but it remains unclear which molecular representation to use. We present a systematic benchmark evaluating LLM molecular competence across nine representations and eight chemical tasks. We benchmark 16 LLMs across five model families, including reasoning and non-reasoning variants, chemistry-specialized LLMs, and closed frontier models. Performance is strongly representation-dependent and no single representation wins across tasks, though CML is the best, followed by MolJSON, InChI, and then canonical SMILES. Explicit structured text representations (CML and MolJSON) dominate structural tasks; IUPAC dominates semantic tasks, winning molecule retrieval for all 16 LLMs; and SMILES variants are rarely optimal despite their prevalence in pretraining. Chemistry-specialized models perform well with SMILES at the cost of large degradations with structured text representations, suggesting SMILES-only evaluation rewards specialization that does not generalize. Using LLM-as-a-judge, we find that IUPAC produces the highest fraction of correct molecule generations. A mechanistic study via tokenization audits, linear probes and attention shows that representations are encoded differently inside the model; for example, structured representations require higher attention across the molecular span. Our results argue against representation-invariant evaluation and motivate task-aware representation routing for LLM-based chemistry.

### [204] [Learn When and Where to Connect: Adaptive Virtual Nodes for Dynamic Message Passing on Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03068)
*Jaejun Lee,Joyce Jiyoung Whang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MAVN是一种端到端可微的MPNN框架，通过动态引入虚拟节点（VNs）并自适应地决定连接时机与对象，克服了传统VN方法在连接数量、固定连接和独立连接等方面的局限。它基于双视角评分机制，在候选VN池中选择每层所需的VN，并实现灵活的节点-VN连接，理论上可模拟任意连接模式。实验表明，MAVN在9个真实数据集上显著提升骨干MPNN性能，最高提升达46.5%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于虚拟节点（VNs）的方法存在三大局限：强制所有节点连接相同数量的VNs、固定连接关系且无法随层调整、节点与VNs的连接相互独立，缺乏对连接重要性的动态评估。因此需要一种更灵活、自适应的框架来优化消息传递过程。

Method: MAVN提出一种端到端可微的MPNN架构，允许非约束性节点-VN连接，动态按需引入虚拟节点。其核心是基于双视角评分机制（节点对VNs的偏好 + VNs对节点的偏好），从候选池中选择每层所需VNs，并仅将其连接至非空子集节点，同时根据连接重要性自适应决定引入时机。

Result: 在9个真实世界数据集上的实验表明，MAVN能持续提升各类骨干MPNN模型的性能，相比基线模型最高提升达46.5%，且优于现有方法。

Conclusion: MAVN通过动态、自适应地引入和连接虚拟节点，实现了更高效的消息传递机制；理论证明其具备模拟任意节点-VN连接模式的能力，实验证明其在多种任务中具有显著优势。

Abstract: While Virtual Nodes (VNs) are often utilized in Message Passing Neural Networks (MPNNs) to facilitate effective message passing, existing VN-based methods have limitations, such as constraining all nodes to connect to the same number of VNs, fixing the connections before applying MPNNs, and connecting a node to a VN independently of the other nodes that connect to the same VN. We propose MAVN, an end-to-end differentiable MPNN framework that allows non-constrained connections between nodes and VNs and dynamically introduces VNs on demand in response to evolving node representations across layers. Specifically, MAVN learns to adaptively determine when (at which layer) and where (to which nodes) to introduce and connect VNs based on the relative importance of connections. From a pool of candidate VNs, MAVN selects the necessary VNs in each layer, where each selected VN is connected to a nonempty subset of nodes, guided by a dual-perspective scoring mechanism that jointly captures the nodes' preferences for VNs and the VNs' preferences for nodes. We theoretically prove that for any node-VN connectivity pattern, there exists a set of MAVN's parameters that can simulate the pattern. Experiments on nine real-world datasets demonstrate that MAVN consistently improves the performance of backbone MPNNs, achieving up to 46.5% improvement over the backbones and outperforms the baselines.

</details>


### [205] [ASymPO: Asymmetric-Scale Policy Optimization for Asynchronous LLM Post-Training Without Behavior Information](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03070)
*Zehua Liu,Yuxuan Yao,Xiaojin Fu,Tao Zhong,Mingxuan Yuan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究异步强化学习在语言模型后训练中的应用，提出一种仅使用当前策略概率的稳定方法ASymPO，以解决因过时响应导致的分布漂移问题。传统方法依赖行为策略概率和重要性权重，但需严格对齐与数值一致性。作者发现存在尺度不平衡问题，即不同响应的损失项在负对数概率尺度上不一致，导致零和优势不再平衡。为此，ASymPO通过归一化每个响应的词元损失来修复该问题，无需行为策略信息，恢复了响应级别的零和平衡并保持非零学习信号。同时引入基线方法SPO，并在异步数学推理后训练中评估了这些仅基于当前策略的目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 异步强化学习可提升语言模型后训练的吞吐量，但过时响应会引发分布漂移。现有行为修正方法依赖复杂且难以保证一致性的行为策略概率，因此亟需一种更鲁棒、无需行为策略信息的替代方案。

Method: 提出Asymmetric-Scale Policy Optimization (ASymPO)，通过将每个响应的词元损失除以其当前平均词元负对数概率来实现尺度归一化，从而缓解尺度不平衡问题；同时设计SPO作为负缩放基线方法进行对比。

Result: ASymPO在异步数学推理后训练任务中表现出良好稳定性，有效恢复响应级零和平衡，保持非零学习信号，且无需行为策略概率，显著降低系统复杂性。

Conclusion: 仅使用当前策略概率即可实现稳定的异步组相对强化学习，ASymPO通过尺度归一化成功解决了传统方法中的尺度不平衡问题，为高效、低耦合的异步训练提供了新范式。

Abstract: Asynchronous reinforcement learning can improve language-model post-training throughput by decoupling response generation from policy optimization, but stale responses introduce distribution drift. Standard behavior-corrected methods control this drift with behavior-policy probabilities, importance ratios, or clipping, which requires token-aligned, versioned, and numerically consistent behavior log-probabilities across rollout and learner systems. We ask whether asynchronous group-relative RL can instead be stabilized using only current-policy probabilities. We identify a scale-imbalance failure mode: when stale responses are evaluated under the current policy, positive and negative loss terms can appear at different negative log-probability scales, so zero-sum advantages no longer imply balanced loss contributions. We propose Asymmetric-Scale Policy Optimization (ASymPO), which normalizes each response's token loss by its current average token negative log-probability. ASymPO requires no behavior-policy probabilities, restores response-level zero-sum balance, and preserves a nonzero learning signal. We also introduce Scaled Policy Optimization (SPO), a fixed negative-scaling baseline, and evaluate both current-policy-only objectives in asynchronous mathematical reasoning post-training.

</details>

In this paper, we propose Joint Fidelity Hyperparameter Optimization (JF-HPO), which simultaneously adapts both model size and training budget as fidelity. JF-HPO is empowered by: (i) it leverages a small proxy model of the target LLM for efficient training and evaluation in each HPO trial; (ii) it integrates carefully designed early-stopping strategies based on training dynamics; (iii) it introduces an efficient checkpointing mechanism to eliminate redundant computations. ### [207] [RMPrior: Bridging Propagation Priors and Diffusion Refinement for Efficient Radio Map Construction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03074)
*Zixuan Guo,Xiucheng Wang,Nan Cheng*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散模型虽能高质量构建无线信道图，但因需从纯噪声逐步去噪，采样开销大，难以适应需频繁刷新的动态无线系统。而传统传播模型蕴含丰富的场景级知识，但标准扩散推理中被完全忽略。因此亟需融合先验知识以减少冗余计算，提升效率与精度。

Method: 提出中段启动采样策略：将匹配的传播先验扰动至某一中间扩散时间步，随后仅执行剩余反向步骤，使模型聚焦于多径感知的精细化修正而非从零重建。利用预训练扩散主干网络完成部分反向过程，实现高效且高质量的重建。

Result: 在IRTF4HighRes数据集上，当$P_{\text{start}}=0.5$时，方法实现2.01倍加速，同时在NMSE、RMSE、SSIM和PSNR四项指标上均优于全步基线。不同传播模型的对比实验显示重建质量与先验质量正相关，且在较短反向路径下对先验质量更敏感，符合理论预测。此外，中段启动的重建质量可有效反映传播模型的场景级保真度。

Conclusion: 本工作成功实现了传播先验与扩散精修的协同，通过中段启动策略显著降低采样开销并提升重建性能。理论与实验共同验证了其有效性，且重建质量可作为传播模型质量的评估代理，为动态无线系统中的高效高保真信道图构建提供了新范式。

Abstract: Diffusion models achieve high-fidelity radio map construction through iterative denoising, yet their sampling cost limits practicality in dynamic wireless systems where radio maps must be refreshed repeatedly. Meanwhile, classical propagation models encode valuable scene-level knowledge that standard diffusion inference discards entirely by initializing from pure Gaussian noise. This paper bridges propagation priors and diffusion refinement through a mid-start sampling strategy. A matched propagation prior is perturbed to an intermediate diffusion timestep, and the pretrained diffusion backbone executes only the remaining reverse steps, focusing computation on multipath-aware refinement rather than full reconstruction from noise. We provide theoretical analysis establishing an upper bound on the initialization gap, a sufficient condition under which truncation improves reconstruction fidelity, and a formal characterization of prior-quality sensitivity under aggressive truncation. Experiments on IRT4HighRes show that, at $P_{\text{start}}=0.5$, the proposed method achieves a $2.01\times$ speedup while simultaneously improving NMSE, RMSE, SSIM, and PSNR over the full-step baseline. A prior-quality ablation across three propagation models of different fidelity confirms that reconstruction quality tracks prior quality, with the sensitivity amplified under shorter reverse trajectories, consistent with the theoretical predictions. These results also suggest that mid-start reconstruction quality can serve as a proxy for ranking the scene-level fidelity of different propagation models.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has become a standard post-training paradigm for large language models (LLMs), extending beyond preference alignment to complex reasoning and multi-turn agentic behaviors. In agentic RL, the rollout stage generates trajectories while invoking tools, producing long-tailed and non-stationary workloads that challenge conventional resource-management assumptions. Three fundamental challenges arise. First, due to the long-tail distribution, a small fraction of trajectories dominates rollout makespan. Second, rollout and training exhibit strong asymmetry in compute patterns, memory demands, and sensitivity to sequence length. Third, as the RL policy evolves, the trajectory-length distribution drifts over time, rendering any static resource split progressively suboptimal.
  We present Libra, which introduces two core mechanisms. The first is a periodic global resource planner that jointly optimizes GPU allocation across rollout and training clusters. It leverages an elastic hybrid pool to enable lightweight, non-blocking worker reallocation between stages. The second is a causality-driven multi-level feedback queue (C-MLFQ) scheduler, which routes requests to heterogeneous rollout buckets based on causal signals derived from tool-return outcomes, rather than relying on fragile length predictions. Evaluated on 48 A800 GPUs, Libra achieves up to 3.0$\times$ higher throughput and converges up to 2.5$\times$ faster in reward compared to the baselines.

Abstract: Causal tracing systematically intervenes on a large language model's (LLM's) internal representations to uncover and quantify the causal pathways linking specific inputs or computations to specific metrics of interest, quantifying the LLM's behavior. Building on previous single-component or single-layer studies, this paper presents a unified framework for causally tracing multiple components simultaneously. This framework systematically identifies the subsets of components (e.g., attention heads and multi-layer perceptron neurons) most critical to a desired target performance metric (e.g., accuracy and fairness). This is achieved by incorporating flexible interventions applied to a wide range of desired metrics. To address the combinatorial complexity of the multi-component problem, an efficient algorithm is designed that leverages soft interventions and a carefully designed metric transformation, converting the combinatorial search problem into a continuous one that can be solved efficiently under proper constraints, thereby generating proper binary decisions for selecting components. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed method efficiently identifies subsets of the model's components that have a high impact on the target metric, outperforming existing baseline approaches. Our code is available at https://github.com/ZiruiYan/multi-component-causal-tracing.

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) improves the ability of large language model, yet headline accuracy gains often conceal a hidden cost: previously solved problems quietly become unsolvable as training proceeds. We frame this phenomenon as \emph{correct-set turnover}, representing the coupled dynamics of solution acquisition and regression over the mastered set. Under this view, retention becomes an explicit optimization target alongside acquisition. We analytically and empirically establish the \emph{repair-window principle}: the cost of restoring a regressed prompt grows sharply with review delay, defining a low-cost window that standard RLVR pipelines fail to exploit. Abstract: On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) has emerged as an efficient post-training paradigm by using a teacher conditioned on privileged information to provide dense token-level supervision. Prior work has shown that OPSD can collapse in verifiable reasoning tasks, but safety alignment differs in that it is guided by high-level constitutions rather than explicit target answers, making it a natural setting to revisit dense distillation. However, our pilot study show that safety OPSD still suffers from severe collapse: constitutional conditioning contracts the teacher distribution toward short and overly conservative responses, and Reverse KL further amplifies this contraction into reduced expressiveness. We formalize this effect as geometric leakage under safety boundaries in a non-orthogonal semantic space, where safety pressure transfers into the expressiveness dimension. Based on this analysis, we propose Constitutional On-Policy Safe Distillation (COPSD), which first calibrates the teacher through a Cross-SFT cold-start and then performs constitution-conditioned on-policy distillation. Motivation: 解决集中式GRPO在分布式数据所有者间部署时面临的数据隐私风险，以及异构任务导致的奖励尺度差异引发的训练不稳定问题。

Result: FGRPO在非独立同分布数据上实现了稳定收敛，有效应对异构任务中的奖励尺度差异，并在保护数据隐私的前提下完成推理模型的高效微调。

Conclusion: FGRPO成功实现了去中心化、高隐私保护的推理模型微调，在异构数据场景下具备良好的稳定性和可扩展性。

Abstract: Recent advances in language models have established reinforcement learning as the primary paradigm for eliciting self-correction and long-chain reasoning. While group relative policy optimization (GRPO) offers superior scalability by eliminating the critic network, deploying it on a central infrastructure entails collecting a large volume of data from distributed owners, which poses significant privacy risks. To address these concerns, we introduce federated GRPO (FGRPO), a framework designed to decentralize the fine-tuning of reasoning models across heterogeneous data owners. To effectively mitigate the instability caused by divergent reward scales across heterogeneous tasks, FGRPO incorporates an adaptive aggregation mechanism based on relative performance gain. By characterizing each client's improvement relative to its personalized historical baseline, the framework dynamically prioritizes effective learning trajectories regardless of local task difficulty. FGRPO ensures robust convergence on non-IID data while preserving data privacy.

Method: 提出G$^2$AT：基于时序密度和表示一致性自适应划分时间序列为高上下文一致性片段；提出FADE：建模细粒度异步跨通道依赖并融合长期历史信息。

Abstract: Multivariate time series forecasting plays a critical role in real-world applications, including weather prediction, stock analysis, and health monitoring. Such irregularities lead to complex and asynchronous temporal dependencies across channels. Thus, a single model with a fixed patching scheme often fails to adapt well to diverse multivariate time series, hindering accurate forecasting. In this paper, we propose TiWeaver, a unified framework designed to handle temporal dynamics and fine-grained inter-channel dependencies adaptively. Specifically, we introduce a Graph-Guided Adaptive Tokenizer (G$^2$AT) that divides time series into high contextually coherent patches by jointly considering temporal density and representation consistency. In addition, we propose a Fine-grained Asynchronous Dependency Extractor (FADE), which is designed to model fine-grained asynchronous inter-channel dependencies while incorporating long-term historical dependencies. We evaluate TiWeaver on 12 real-world time series datasets, where it achieves state-of-the-art performance, outperforming existing methods up to 25%. ### [215] [Synthetic Hallucinations, Real Gains: Hard Negatives from Frontier Models for FIM Hallucination Mitigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03130)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从公共GitHub抓取多语言FIM上下文，使用三个前沿代码生成器为每种上下文生成四种类型（基于Delulu分类）的硬负例；构建配对的‘选择/拒绝’数据集；基于此数据集对Qwen2.5-Coder系列模型进行监督微调（SFT），并评估其在多个基准上的表现。

Conclusion: 本方法提供了一种高效、可扩展且无需执行的幻觉缓解策略，通过合成硬负例实现有效监督信号，显著提升代码补全质量，并开放完整工具链以促进研究复现与推广。

Abstract: Small open-source code models that power IDE autocomplete still emit hallucinated Fill-in-the-Middle (FIM) completions: syntactically natural calls to methods, parameters, variables, and imports that do not exist in the surrounding project. Existing mitigations either require per-language execution sandboxes that do not apply at mid-keystroke or preference-optimisation pipelines that need large human-labelled corpora. We propose an execution-free alternative: use frontier code models to synthesise plausible-but-wrong completions as hard negatives, then leverage the contrast between these synthetic hallucinations and the ground-truth developer edit as a supervised fine-tuning signal. Our pipeline scrapes multilingual FIM contexts from public GitHub across eight languages and asks a panel of three frontier generators to produce one hard negative per context for each of four hallucination types drawn from the Delulu taxonomy, a Docker-verified multilingual FIM hallucination benchmark, yielding a paired chosen/rejected dataset. Fine-tuning Qwen2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct on a 100K-row curated subset lifts Delulu exact match by +18.8 points and edit similarity by +0.22 on every language and every type, while also improving every HumanEval-Infilling split and every SAFIM subset. The same recipe at 3B lifts Delulu by +12.8 EM with a small, characterised general-FIM trade-off. Five-axis ablations (size, type mix, language coverage, base-model family, and a difficulty-aware fool rate) plus a head-to-head SFT vs. DPO/ORPO comparison map which design choices drive the gain. We release the full pipeline source code -- generation, fool-rate LLM judging, curation, and the FIM fine-tuning recipe -- so that the experiments in this paper can be reproduced end-to end on any permissively licensed corpus.

Method: HARVE方法从残差流方向中识别与特定劫持子类相关的多方向劫持子空间，通过移除奖励头向量中与该子空间对齐的分量来降低对劫持特征的敏感性，仅需少量对比黄金样本，无梯度更新或微调过程。

Abstract: Reward models are central to large language model (LLM) alignment, but they remain vulnerable to reward hacking. To mitigate these failures, we propose HARVE, a training-free reward-head editing method for scalar reward models. Instead of fine-tuning the reward model, HARVE identifies a multi-directional hacking subspace from residual stream directions associated with selected hacking subcategories, and removes the component of the reward-head vector aligned with that subspace. This directly reduces the reward head's sensitivity to hacking-related features using only a small set of contrastive gold-hacked examples, without gradient updates or fine-tuning. Comprehensive experiments across eight reward models indicates that \model improves hacking robustness, outperforms fine-tuning baselines, and preserves reward-models' general capability. Further analyses suggest that reward hacking is better captured as a multidimensional residual-space structure than by isolated surface cues.

While cross-user collaboration can overcome this data bottleneck, current trajectory-sharing approaches compromise user privacy and impose a uniform global library that fails to accommodate client heterogeneity. We introduce FederatedSkill, a privacy-preserving framework for collaborative agent evolution. TL;DR: Clari is a fast, scalable flow matching model for organic crystal structure prediction (CSP) that generates unit cells in seconds, surpassing OXtal in solve rate and speed. It uses atom types and bonds as input, supports explicit hydrogens, enables energy-based ranking without relaxation, and works on complex chemistries like fullerenes and metal complexes. It introduces a new benchmark set (CSD Teaching Subset) and achieves 5–30× speedup.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

While generative models like OXtal reduce this cost, they still suffer from high computational overhead due to triangle layers and lack of efficient parametrization. There is a need for faster, more generalizable, and accurate CSP methods enabling large-scale virtual screening.

Method: Clari employs a large-scale flow matching model that generates redundancy-free unit cells using pure pair-bias attention instead of triangle layers. It operates directly on atom types and bonds without requiring RDKit-sanitized molecules, and explicitly models hydrogen atoms to enable direct energy ranking during inference.

Result: Clari achieves a 15–30× speedup over OXtal on test sets, improves solve rate, and maintains a 5–8× speedup when generating 150 crystals and selecting top-30 by energy. It successfully handles challenging systems such as fullerenes and metal complexes. The CSD Teaching Subset is introduced as a new benchmark for diverse, complex molecules.

Abstract: Organic crystal structure prediction (CSP) is a requirement for computational modelling of organic solids, but traditionally costs several CPU-years per molecule. Generative models such as OXtal dramatically reduce this cost by sampling stable organic crystal structures directly. However, OXtal forgoes explicit lattice parametrization in favour of modelling large crops of the bulk material with expensive triangle layers, which can incur a computational cost of minutes per molecule. In this paper, we reduce this to seconds with Clari, a large-scale flow matching model that generates redundancy-free unit cells and replaces triangle layers with pure pair-bias attention. Clari requires only atom types and bonds as input and does not need an RDKit-sanitizable input molecule, which expands its applicability to challenging chemistries such as fullerenes, metal complexes, and atom clusters. We further ablate key design choices such as auxiliary losses, timestep distributions, noise priors, and self-conditioning. On OXtal's test sets, we surpass OXtal's solve rate while obtaining a speedup of $15$-$30\times$. Because Clari also models explicit hydrogens, it supports inference-time scaling via direct energy ranking, without any decoration or relaxation step. When generating 150 crystals and selecting the top-30 by energy, we further improve solve rate while maintaining a speedup of $5$-$8\times$. We also introduce the CSD Teaching Subset as a new test split of diverse and complex molecules for future benchmarking. Our contributions enable CSP within seconds, making large-scale virtual screening of organic solids practical. Code is available at https://github.com/aspuru-guzik-group/clari.

### [219] [DECA: Decentralizing Block-Wise Adam for Efficient LLM Full-Parameter Fine-Tuning on Non-IID Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03209)
*Yunsheng Yuan,Shaowei Li,Kai Wang,Zhongyuan Sun,Zheng Zhang,Kai Han,Jun Luo,Feng Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DECA 是一种资源高效的去中心化全参数微调框架，适用于非独立同分布（non-IID）数据下的大语言模型。通过将模型参数分块并进行分块顺序 Adam 优化，DECA 在保持全参数适应能力的同时显著降低资源消耗。此外，引入一阶和二阶分块动量估计及本地梯度统计与共识差异信号，有效稳定训练过程。理论分析与实验均表明，DECA 具有快速收敛、优异下游性能和显著资源效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在隐私敏感和资源受限环境下对大语言模型进行微调仍具挑战性。由于训练数据分布在多个客户端，去中心化微调成为无需中央服务器的协作适应自然范式。然而，全参数微调在去中心化设置中资源消耗巨大，现有方法多依赖参数高效更新，虽提升效率但可能限制下游性能；同时，客户端数据通常为非独立同分布，导致优化易受客户端漂移和收敛不稳定影响。

Method: DECA 将模型参数划分为互不重叠的块，采用分块顺序 Adam 优化策略，降低资源开销同时保留全参数微调能力。引入基于本地新梯度统计的一阶与二阶动量估计，以及由共识推导出的差异信号，以增强训练稳定性。

Result: 实验与理论分析表明，DECA 实现了快速收敛、强下游性能和显著资源效率，优于现有方法，在非 IID 数据下表现稳健。

Conclusion: DECA 成功实现了资源高效的去中心化全参数微调，在非 IID 数据场景下兼顾性能与效率，为大语言模型在分布式环境中的实际应用提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Fine-tuning large language models (LLMs) in privacy-sensitive and resource-constrained environments remains challenging. Since training data are often distributed across multiple clients, decentralized fine-tuning offers a natural paradigm for collaborative adaptation without a central server. However, enabling full-parameter fine-tuning (FPFT) in this decentralized setting is difficult: FPFT provides strong adaptation capacity but incurs prohibitive resource consumption for billion-scale models. Existing decentralized LLM fine-tuning methods therefore mainly rely on parameter-efficient updates, which improve efficiency but may restrict downstream performance. Moreover, client data are typically non-IID, making decentralized optimization more vulnerable to client drift and unstable convergence. To address these challenges, we propose DECA, a resource-efficient decentralized FPFT framework for LLMs on non-IID data. DECA partitions model parameters into disjoint blocks and performs sequential block-wise Adam optimization, reducing resource consumption while preserving decentralized full-parameter adaptation. To stabilize training, DECA further introduces first- and second-order block-wise moment estimates with fresh local gradient statistics and consensus-derived discrepancy signals. We provide rigorous theoretical analysis and extensive experiments, showing that DECA achieves fast convergence, strong downstream performance, and significant resource efficiency.

</details>


### [220] [Bayesian Tensor Decomposition with Diffusion Model Prior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03212)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有低秩张量分解在严重缺失或噪声下表现不佳，且传统手工设计先验（如稀疏性、平滑性）难以捕捉真实数据的复杂统计特性。而当前最先进的扩散模型难以与张量分解和可 tractable 后验推断兼容，因此需要一种能注入数据驱动先验并保持推理可行性的新方法。

Method: 提出DiffBCP框架，融合累积收缩过程先验用于自动选择张量分解秩，同时利用预训练扩散模型作为隐式数据先验。设计分裂吉布斯采样器：CP因子采用共轭更新，扩散部分通过低秩引导的去噪进行采样。引入噪声自适应耦合调度以减少对人工退火参数的敏感性。

Result: 在图像补全与去噪任务中，包括高分辨率分布外图像，DiffBCP在多个指标上均显著优于现有的贝叶斯、非线性及插件式张量分解基线方法，显示出更强的鲁棒性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: DiffBCP成功将预训练扩散模型融入张量分解框架，通过数据驱动的隐式先验提升在严重损坏条件下的恢复性能，同时保持后验推断的可行性，为张量分解在真实世界复杂数据中的应用提供了新范式。

Abstract: Low-rank tensor decomposition (TD) is usually effective on clean, fully observed data, but it often degrades under severe missingness or noise. Low-rankness is itself a useful but limited structural prior, and additional handcrafted priors (e.g., sparsity or smoothness) still fall short of capturing the rich statistics of real-world data. To compensate for this weak inductive bias under heavy corruption, one would like to inject a learned, data-driven prior; however, the state-of-the-art diffusion models are not readily compatible with current TD and tractable posterior inference. To address these challenges, we introduce DiffBCP, a hybrid-prior Bayesian CP decomposition framework that couples a cumulative shrinkage process prior over the CP factors for automatic rank selection with an off-the-shelf pre-trained diffusion model as an implicit data prior on the reconstructed tensor. To make posterior inference tractable despite the coupling among the likelihood, low-rank constraint, and diffusion prior, we develop a split Gibbs sampler: CP factors admit conjugate updates, while the diffusion block is sampled via low-rank-guided denoising. A noise-adaptive coupling schedule further reduces sensitivity to hand-tuned annealing. Experiments on image inpainting and denoising, including high-resolution out-of-distribution images, show consistent gains over Bayesian, nonlinear, and plug-and-play TD baselines.

</details>
